Special Essay

A Study on the Transplantation of Korean People to the Northeast

(Continued from the previous article) Bin

(III) Historical Examination of the Transplantation of Korean People to the Northeast

The transplantation of Korean people to the Northeast is not a recent event. Its historical evolution is of great importance to this issue. We should urgently trace its origins to understand the historical progress of this issue and use it as a reference for resolving it. However, our country's historical records and ancient books often neglect border issues, and there is even less information on the transplantation of Korean people to our land. As for the Japanese side, they fabricate historical facts and make far-fetched interpretations. For example, Yano and others have even written special books, claiming that the Northeast is not our country's territory. These kinds of absurd arguments are intended to confuse international opinion and benefit their acts of aggression. If we are not careful, we will be deceived and used by them without realizing it. For example, the Japanese also fabricate much of the historical fact of the transplantation of Korean people to our Northeast or deliberately make biased statements. If our countrymen do not examine them carefully and take them as a basis, they will spread errors and fall into their conspiracies, causing great mistakes. This is what we must pay close attention to when examining historical facts.

According to more reliable records in recent times, the transplantation of Korean people to our Northeast began after the early years of Guangxu. Before that, although there were Korean people who crossed the border to steal and cultivate land, it was not a formal transplantation. Wu Luzhen's "Report on Border Affairs in Yanji," compiled in the thirty-third year of Guangxu of the Qing Dynasty, states:

"When the Qing Dynasty established its rule in the Central Plains, Korea was listed as a vassal state. The way of paying tribute, exchanging envoys, and conducting trade was generally by crossing the Yalu River from Uiju in Korea and reaching Fengcheng in Shengjing. As for the area north of the Tumen River, it was a key area for the Qing Dynasty's foundation and was completely sealed off. The ban on illegal immigrants entering the country was extremely strict. Reading the clear edict of the early Qing Dynasty banning Jilin and the strict decree of patrolling the Tumen River in the years of Daoguang, it is clear that the people were extinct here for two hundred years, and Koreans even more so. In the early Qing Dynasty, the border between Jilin and Korea was extremely strict. If the people of the two countries privately crossed the Tumen River by one step, they would be executed by officials of the two countries, or they would be killed without exception. Therefore, not only were Korean people not allowed to cross the river, but also Chinese people who crossed the river without reason were clearly violating the strict ban."

This shows that in the early days of the Qing Dynasty, the three northeastern provinces were regarded as their birthplace, and the residence of people was prohibited, especially to prevent the transplantation of Korean people. The border between China and Korea was extremely strict. Koreans were not allowed to cross the river to violate our territory, and our people were not allowed to cross one step privately. The Yalu River was like a natural moat. This is a verifiable historical fact. However, the Japanese deliberately said that since the early Qing Dynasty, the area between Baishan and Heishui had become a vast wilderness without belonging. We can easily see what their words are intended for.

In the ninth year of Tongzhi, there was heavy rain and hail in Korea, and the country was extremely barren. Hungry people filled the roads. Korean people did not hesitate to violate the heavy ban, crossed the river and border, sold their wives and children, and begged for food. However, within a year, the Korean people who had families still returned to their homeland. Those who stayed in China were only male servants and female slaves. (At this time, in Hunchun and other places in Jilin, one son or one daughter of a Korean person could be exchanged for a bucket of rice.) At that time, there were only Korean people who were employed as servants and lived on food, but there were no Korean people who cultivated land across the border. In the early years of Guangxu, Dunhua County released wasteland and investigated land. There were Korean people who privately cultivated land in places such as Wailiudaogou, opposite Mount Mu in Korea. This was because the area near Hunchun was patrolled by troops sent by the assistant commander every year. Those who privately reclaimed fields and built houses were destroyed. However, places opposite Mount Mu were farther away from Hunchun, and patrols were slightly neglected. However, although there were Korean people who risked the ban to steal and cultivate land at that time, there were no Korean people who received wasteland to cultivate. The violation and intrusion of Korean people were by no means a formal transplantation.

In the seventh year of Guangxu, the Jilin General Ming'an supervised border defense. Wu Dacheng was approved to investigate the household registration of Korean refugees and assign them to the jurisdiction of Hunchun and Dunhua. It was not until this time that Korean people began to receive wasteland and rent land in our Yanbian territory. However, they had no land sovereignty at all. The Korean emperor was afraid of the emigration of his people and even asked our country to return the refugees. The document sent to the Ministry of Rites stated:

Martial Law Declared in Beiping and Tianjin

▲Yu Xuezhong and Zhang Xueming Appointed as Commanders of Martial Law

Beiping Correspondence: After the military action on the Pinghan Railway, the Beiping and Tianjin Garrison Command, in order to ensure local security, issued a martial law order on the 20th, with Yu Xuezhong concurrently serving as commander, and appointed Shao Wenkai, deputy commander of the military police, and Bao Yulin, director of the Public Security Bureau, as deputy commanders. The original text of the martial law order is as follows: "Considering that Shi Yousan's troops are prone to creating disturbances"

"and are planning to rebel, in order to protect the security of Beiping, a martial law order should be issued to remove obstacles and pacify the area. In addition to the commander of Beiping Martial Law being concurrently held by this commander, Shao Wenkai, deputy commander of the military police, and Bao Yulin, director of the Beiping Public Security Bureau, are appointed as deputy commanders of Beiping Martial Law, and after reporting and distributing, the martial law regulations are hereby announced for the military, civilians, and others to abide by. This order." Martial Law Regulations: (1) Prohibit gatherings, associations, strikes, market closures, or news magazines, books, and various printed materials that are deemed detrimental to military affairs. (2) Civilian goods that can be used for military needs may be prohibited from being exported if necessary. (3) Inspect privately owned firearms, ammunition, weapons, fire tools, and other dangerous goods, and confiscate or confiscate them if necessary. (4) Inspect postal letters and telegrams. (5) Inspect export ships and other goods, or stop land and water transportation when necessary. (6) Supervise and guide local militia and peasant groups. If there are illegal acts in various groups that hinder military operations, they may be ordered to disarm and disband at any time. (7) When destruction of people's real estate is unavoidable due to combat, appropriate compensation should be given. (8) Within the martial law area, day or night, when necessary, homes, buildings, shops, ships, etc. may be inspected. (9) People residing in the martial law area may be ordered to withdraw when necessary. (10) When it is deemed that the martial law situation has ended, a declaration of解除戒嚴 (jiechu jieyan) lifting of martial law will be made. Commander Yu Xuezhong, July 19, the 20th year of the Republic of China.

Tianjin News: Regarding the implementation of martial law in Tianjin, according to a statement from a certain person in the Second Army Command, regarding the implementation of martial law and the problem of maintaining public security in Tianjin and Beiping, Tianjin originally planned to have Wang Shuchang as the commander-in-chief of martial law and Zhang Xueming as the deputy commander. Later, Deputy Commander Zhang believed that Wang still had to take on the frontline command, so it has been decided to appoint Tianjin Mayor Zhang Xueming as the commander-in-chief of martial law, with Guo Dianju, brigade commander of the Fourteenth Brigade, as the deputy commander, to strengthen prevention. Mayor Zhang has received an order from the executive headquarters. The city's Public Security Bureau is currently preparing for martial law. After Mayor Zhang returns to Tianjin from Beiping and meets with Deputy Commander Guo, the Martial Law Headquarters can be officially established. (21st)

Fu Shuangying's Talk on the Current Situation

Taiyuan Correspondence: The circumstances of Fu Shuangying's visit to Bing have been reported in previous newspapers. The mission of Fu's visit is: (1) to inspect the situation in Shanxi; (2) to convey the intentions of Chiang and Zhang; (3) to solicit the opinions of various generals on the current situation. In the past two days, Fu visited various parties and exchanged opinions, which was very harmonious. The Shanxi generals Shang Zhen, Yang Aiyuan, Sun Chu, Song Zheyuan, Pang Bingxun, Fu Zuoyi, Rong Honglu, Zhang Huizhao, Zhou Dai, Li Shengda, Li Fuying, Yang Chengyuan, Yang Xiaoou, Feng Pengzhu, Yang Yaofang, Wang Jingguo, Zhao Chengshou, Li Runfa, etc., specially held a joint banquet at the Shanxi Hotel last night.

To welcome Fu and to remove the dust, after the banquet, a lengthy agreement was reached on the current situation. Fu's attitude was extremely optimistic. The reporter visited yesterday and recorded his conversation as follows: (Reporter asked) When did the military commander arrive in Shanxi? Fu (replied) I arrived here at 4:10 pm on the 16th of this month. (Asked) Can you tell us about the commander's experiences over the years? (Answered) I have been in the military for about 20 years, and have served as a brigade commander and military commander.

Page 11

In various battles, I am ashamed of my lack of achievements due to my limited talent and strength. Since the reorganization, I originally intended to return to the fields and recuperate, but I was entrusted by Vice-Chairman Zhang to be a military advisor, and last winter I was ordered to take over the Jingxing Mining Bureau. I have a great interest in industrial affairs, because the suffering of the people in our country for more than ten years has been unbearable. If I can contribute to a little production enterprise for the society, it would be much better than the dangers of war and would benefit a lot. I will study mining affairs carefully and gradually develop it, but whether I can achieve my wish can only be left to fate. (Asked) What is the mission of your visit? (Answered) I came here because the generals in Shanxi are mostly classmates and old friends. I was instructed by the Deputy Commander to come here to convey the overall situation in the North. It is more important to unite and reorganize than to destroy. Moreover, every man has a responsibility for the rise and fall of the country. At this critical moment of internal and external troubles, we soldiers are particularly important. The Third International is doing everything possible to provoke and destroy, and will not stop until China is no longer a country. How should we be responsible for prevention? If there are elements who are used by them, we should work together to drive out evil and support what is right, abandon selfishness and value righteousness, in order to maintain the national interest. How can we harm the people with selfish intentions? It is much better to conserve strength and build up energy to face the outside world with great courage than to engage in civil war in the country. I came here only based on this purpose. Fortunately, all the generals can meet each other with sincerity, and I am quite optimistic about the future of the overall situation. Regarding the Shanxi and Northwest armies, since the reorganization last year, it has been a complete plan, and they all belong to the same army, so there is no difference in treatment. Therefore, the Deputy Commander has repeatedly asked the Central Government to maintain the various armies at all costs to prevent disasters and consolidate the country. However, due to the hasty time and insufficient preparation, it was not possible to fulfill the wish immediately. Now that a considerable amount of time has passed, all the departments that have been announced and established will be treated the same as the Northeast, without any favoritism. Finally, he also said that although the Deputy Commander is only about thirty years old, he is extremely loyal and sincere in treating people, and often says that he can be friends with anyone and can be used by anyone. If someone tells him that someone is not good, he will say that it is his own fault, that he is not sincere enough to impress people, and that he is not wise enough to observe people. What can he blame others for? From this, we can see his character. As for the Vice Chairman's illness, he has now recovered and is currently in a period of recuperation. He will be discharged from the hospital in a few days and often meets with guests and news reporters to talk, but according to the doctor's advice, the talk time should be short and not too long. He had intended to go to Beidaihe for recuperation, but after persuasion from all parties, he is still recuperating in the hospital, which is more suitable than going to Beidaihe. He has now decided to recuperate in the hospital and will no longer go to Beidaihe. Fu also telegraphed Hou Zhencun, the director of the Jingxing Mining Bureau, yesterday, saying that at this time when rumors are rampant, the bureau's staff and workers should remain calm and work, and invited them to come to Jin to discuss everything. It can be seen that Fu's attitude is also quite calm.

Wanbaoshan Becomes a Japanese Alert Zone

▲Japanese Police Actually Expel Original Chinese Residents

Recent news from Jilin: Yesterday, someone came from Wanbaoshan to the province to report that as of the 14th, the Japanese, under supervision, directed Korean people and Shandong workers to dig through the ditches that had been leveled by the civilians before, and set up a total of 29 cloth tents. In the tents, a Japanese flag was erected high. Within three miles, our people were still not allowed to pass through, so the area had become a Japanese alert zone. Many people's houses have been occupied. So far, the negotiations on this case have been such that we have no way to expel the illegal occupying Koreans, while they have actually expelled the original Chinese residents, making it impossible for them to stay. The injustice of the matter is such.

The Wanbaoshan case in Changchun was originally a matter that could be resolved locally, but the Japanese side was unilaterally strong and overbearing, and carried new-style artillery to put too much pressure on us. Our people still know that the country is important and have never dared to confront the Japanese police directly, but sometimes they took advantage of their carelessness to dig through the soil and fill the moats, hoping to restore the original state of the farmland. When they saw the Japanese police coming, they fled and dispersed. Their plight is also pitiful. Unexpectedly, they are still arguing strongly and making alarming statements about one or two small things. For example, at noon on the 12th of this month, students from the Changchun Commercial Port Elementary School were giving speeches about the Wanbaoshan incident in the old city market. A Japanese military police officer, Inoue, disguised himself in Chinese clothes and mocked them from the side. A student, Chi Shirong, only thirteen years old, had a verbal argument with him and tore Inoue's gown. Inoue immediately grabbed the student and claimed that he had lost his watch and official documents. After our Public Security Bureau compensated for the loss, the matter was settled. The Japanese newspapers immediately published a headline, saying that the anti-Japanese trend in Changchun was intensifying, that Japanese military officials were beaten by the people for no reason, and that Japanese residents did not dare to go out. On the 13th, the Japanese consul stationed in Jilin suddenly declared to our authorities that more than 1,000 students in Dunhua were conducting a grand anti-Japanese propaganda campaign, fearing that an ominous event would soon break out. After investigation, it was learned that the commercial and academic circles of Dunhua had received a telegram from the Korean Chinese Chamber of Commerce about the situation of the overseas Chinese being harmed, and a special meeting was held to discuss and telegraph the provincial government for a serious protest, as a diplomatic backing. The Japanese side's creation of troubles has been like this recently.

Mass Rally in Beiping by All Circles to Support Overseas Chinese and Oppose Japan

▲ Resolution to Form a Committee to Support Overseas Chinese and Oppose Japan

Beiping Correspondence: The Beiping mass rally to support overseas Korean Chinese and oppose the Japanese movement was held yesterday (the 20th) at 9:00 AM in the Zhongshan Hall of Zhongshan Park. More than 300 people attended. The presidium consisted of eight people, including Chen Shiquan from the Municipal Party Department, Yang Shaoye from the Chamber of Commerce, Zheng Guocai from the Provincial Party Department, Liu Ying from the Farmers' Association, Zhang Deliu from the PingSui Special Party Department, Zhou Xuechang from the Education Association, Di Yingxian from the Municipal Government, and Hou Fu from the Labor Union. Chen Shiquan served as the Chairman. After the formal opening ceremony, the Chairman reported on the significance of the meeting, saying, in brief, "Today is the Beiping City mass rally to support Korean Chinese and oppose the Japanese movement. We should commemorate it with sorrow and grief. Since the Wanbaoshan Massacre on July 1st, Japan has provoked the emotions between China and Korea, using the Koreans as tools to massacre Chinese living in Korea. We should recognize two points about this: (1) This Korean anti-Chinese massacre was very methodical and was instigated and manipulated by the Japanese. This tragedy is not only heartbreaking for us but also leaves a major stain on human history. The responsibility for this should be borne by Japanese imperialism. (2) We should sympathize with the Chinese victims of the Korean massacre and hope that they realize the need to unite the weak nations' front. This meeting has two major tasks: (1) How to assist the overseas Chinese, and (2) How to resist Japanese imperialism. The overseas Chinese have suffered greatly this time. Our compatriots at home should provide assistance in spirit and materially. Some of our compatriots who suffered have already sacrificed themselves under the iron heel of imperialism. The responsibility of revenge rests on the surviving Chinese. We should urge the government to lodge a serious protest and have the spirit of enduring hardship and persevering. We should unite and resist Japanese imperialism, sever economic relations with it, and have the determination to fight Japanese imperialism to the death. We should not only inform the people of the whole country of this situation but also the people of the world. International propaganda is everyone's responsibility. Finally, we hope that the Koreans realize that the only way to maintain peace is for China and Korea to shake hands." Next, Zheng Guocai reported on the process. Finally, eleven proposals were passed: (1) The Chairman proposed a draft declaration of the conference and asked for its approval. (2) The Presidium proposed to send a telegram to the National Government, asking it to negotiate seriously with Japan and implement effective assistance, together with the draft telegram for approval. (3) The Presidium proposed to send a telegram of condolence to the affected overseas Chinese, together with the draft telegram for approval. (4) The Presidium proposed to send a telegram to the whole country to unite against Japan, together with the draft telegram for approval. (5) The Presidium proposed to issue a letter to the Korean people, together with the draft of the letter, for approval. (6) The Presidium proposed to carry out propaganda to the world to stop Japan's counter-propaganda. (7) The Presidium proposed to organize the Beiping Committee to Support Overseas Korean Chinese and Oppose Japan, responsible for planning and implementing the work of supporting overseas Chinese and opposing Japan, and to recommend the Party Department of Hebei Province, the Party Department of Beiping City, the Party Department of PingSui Railway, the Beiping General Chamber of Commerce, the Beiping Suburban Farmers' Association, the Beiping Education Association, the Beiping Large Vehicle Workers' Union, the Tram Workers' Union, the Newspaper Carriers' Union, the Journalists' Association, the PingSui Railway Union, Peking University, Beijing University, the Oriental Problems Research Association, the Beiping Bankers' Association, the Beiping Preparatory Committee for Autonomy, and other organizations to be members, asking for a public decision. (8) The Preparatory Committee for Autonomy proposed to raise funds to be remitted to Korea to provide relief to the overseas Chinese, with any party advancing the funds first and then being reimbursed after the funds were raised, with the amount being at least 10,000 yuan. (9) Ye Mengyuan proposed to suspend all entertainment in the city for three days. (10) Cui Jingyuan proposed to actively prepare for land reclamation to establish a clear diplomatic policy towards Japan. (11) Dong Lin proposed to send a telegram to warn Shi Yousan and others in Guangdong to lay down their butcher knives and unite against foreign enemies. All the above proposals were unanimously approved. The meeting adjourned at 1:30 PM. (21st)

Shandong Brick, Tile, and Book Exhibition

▲ Tens of Thousands of Visitors on the First Day

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Library, in order to awaken the attention and interest of all circles in preserving antiquities, has specially opened a brick, tile, and book exhibition. Today (21st) is the first day of the public exhibition. The brick and tile exhibition is set up in the reference book reading room on the ground floor of the north building of the library. On display are the Qin and Han bricks and tiles collected by Gao Zang in Weixian County. Numbers one and two are the twelve-character bricks of the Xiongnu peace treaty, one in yangwen (raised characters) and the other in yinwen (recessed characters). The famous twelve-character brick "Hai Nei Jie Chen" (All Subjects Within the Seas) was taken away by Japan. The value of the above two bricks can be compared to that of the Xiongnu. The remaining bricks and tiles, which were previously disclosed, are also on display. Also on display is the book "Shizhong Shanfang Wanyin Lou Yinwen" (Seal Imprints from the Ten Bell Studio and Ten Thousand Seal Building) by Chen Fusai of Weixian County, and "Xiao Pan Lu Zhuanwa Wenzi" (Brick and Tile Texts from the Little Climbing Cottage) edited by Xu Yinlin of Rizhao. The printing plates of Chen's book are kept by the Chen family, and each copy requires a price of over one hundred yuan. Xu's book is currently kept in the library, and the original plates are probably not easy to obtain. These are also on display. In addition, what is eye-catching is the four scrolls written by Li Wanyong of Korea, which are hung on the north wall. One scroll contains a poem that reads, "A hundred battles have won功名, the heavenly troops are full of yìqì, the three borders will never fight永不戰, this is my royal英." Another scroll reads, "Ten thousand miles of plains in Southern Manchuria, the scenery is broad and the autumn sky is vast. The battle迹跡留餘憤, even more cause the traveler to have暗愁." Another scroll reads, "Holy virtue transcends the 千古, royal威静四方, the common people now息戰, feel the long time of無事." Another scroll contains the four characters "Shoushan Fuhai" (Longevity Mountain and Blessed Sea). Under each scroll is the signature Yitang Li Wanyong, with two seals: one is the seal of Li Wanyong, and the other is "Yitang." Wang Xiantang, the librarian, has a postscript, which roughly says that Li Wanyong is a traitor who sold Korea. Our Chinese who sell antiquities to foreigners are also traitors, because antiquities are where the national culture is寄. The book exhibition is set up in the museum under the Hutian Yijiao building. On display are the Song, Yuan, and Ming rare books collected by Haiyuan Pavilion in the cabinet of the Grand Library, too many to be recorded. Also on display are the "You Huang Zuo Xiao Tu" (Seated and Whistling in a Bamboo Grove) and "Xun Chi Chang He Tu" (Ocarina and Panpipe Harmony Picture) made by Yu Zhiding for Wang Yuyang, which are also rare精品. The library has printed a small pamphlet called "Why Should Brick, Tile, and Books be Exhibited," and everyone who signs in at the meeting will receive a copy. The library's quarterly, "Haiyuan Pavilion Zhu Yuan Secret Book Catalogue," "The Present and Future of Haiyuan Pavilion's Collection," and brick and tile images are also sold temporarily. In the morning and afternoon, visitors came in an endless stream, and almost no space was available in the entire library. In total, on the first day, there were about tens of thousands of people. Also, the aforementioned book "Seal Imprints from the Ten Bell Studio and Ten Thousand Seal Building," with the printing plates kept by the Chen family in Weixian County, and the originals are also kept in the Chen family, totaling more than 7,000 ancient seals. In particular, the two seals Zhao Feiyan Seal and Huaiyang Wang Seal are珍寳世. It was previously rumored that the Chen family would sell them to Japanese merchants, asking for 130,000 yuan. The Japanese merchants offered 80,000 yuan, but the Chen family refused. It is now heard that the Japanese merchants are still living in Weixian County, willing to offer 110,000 yuan, intending to get them at all costs, but the deal has not yet been成交. A certain party has now sent a letter to the magistrate of Weixian County, asking him to pay attention to this matter, lest national treasures flow to foreign lands again. (21st)

Investigation of Disaster Situation in Various Counties in Northern Anhui

▲ Various Counties Have Formed Disaster Relief Associations

▲ Appealing to All Parties for Relief

Bengbu Correspondence: The recent floods in northern Anhui have turned the area along the Huai River into a swamp. The disaster area covers more than 20 counties. People who have drowned or starved to death are happening all the time. Property losses are no less than several million. The voices of various counties calling for disaster relief are deafening. A few days ago, the Huai River water level showed a slight pause in rising, but there was no way to discharge it, and the recession was very slow. Unexpectedly, since the 19th, it has been raining again, non-stop. Therefore, the crops, trees, and houses are still mostly in the water. The disaster situation in each county is recorded as follows:

▲ Wuhe: Wuhe's terrain is low-lying. The Huai, Hui, Chong, Tong, and Tuo rivers surround the entire county, making it prone to floods. In recent years, it has suffered repeated poor harvests, and famines have been frequent. This summer, it was hoped that the two wheat crops would have a bumper harvest to alleviate the people's difficulties, but unexpectedly, they were flooded before they matured. After the water receded, the autumn crops were just planted when it rained continuously, and the Huai River flooded. The dikes and embankments were all breached, and a vast expanse of water turned into a swamp. Most of the people's houses collapsed, and they lived in the open air, barely eking out a living. The fields were filled with wailing, crying out for relief. The Wuhe branch of the World Red Swastika Society recently sent telegrams to various Red Swastika Society branches, appealing for the disaster victims.

▲ Fengyang: Fengyang borders the Huai River to the north and has flat terrain. The heavy rain caused the water depth on the flat ground to reach several feet. The autumn crops were completely submerged. Linhuai, due to its proximity to the Huai River and low-lying terrain, had a water depth of nearly ten feet in some places. More than 2,000 households of residents' houses were washed down by the rain. The local Red Swastika Society has also united with all circles to organize a flood emergency relief association to raise relief funds to help the disaster victims.

▲ Suxian: Suxian previously suffered a hailstorm, and the farmers suffered heavy losses. This time, there were four consecutive days of torrential rain, day and night. The water depth in the streets and markets was about a foot, and many houses collapsed. In the Xupoji area of the first district, the water depth on the flat ground was three feet, and boats could travel without obstruction. Moreover, the heavy rain in Yongcheng and Xiayi counties in eastern Henan also flowed into the Suxian border. Therefore, the low-lying areas in the northwest of the county have become a swamp. The autumn crops have been completely submerged. The district chiefs of each district in the county have separately investigated the disaster situation and reported it for relief.

▲ Mengcheng: Mengcheng is located in the Wo River basin, with the Fei River to the north and the Qian River to the south. The soil is fertile, making it the crown of the counties in northern Anhui. Since the beginning of summer, there has been continuous rain, and water has accumulated everywhere, forming ditches. During the recent heavy rain, which lasted for five days and nights, the Wo, Fei, and Qian rivers flooded at the same time, overflowing and mixing together. The water depth on the flat ground was five or six feet, drowning people and animals, and washing down houses, countless. The crops have been completely submerged, and the autumn harvest is almost hopeless. The people are crying out in pain, and the disaster situation is very serious.

▲ Shouxian: Shouxian has been suffering from continuous rain since the beginning of summer. Last month, when the Huai River water rose, the former county magistrate Zhang Xiangkun removed the moat dam outside the north gate of the city, causing the river water to overflow and flood the fields. Recently, there has been torrential rain and flash floods. Several sections of the north and south walls of the county were washed down by the rain, and the city and countryside were a vast expanse of water. Countless fields, houses, people, and livestock were swept away. Zhengyangguan in the southwest, due to its proximity to the confluence of the Huai and Pi rivers, had dangerous water conditions. The city and countryside were submerged in water, and the disaster situation was particularly tragic.

▲ Yingshang: Yingshang is located west of Shouxian, bordering the south bank of the Ying River and north of the Huai River. The terrain is low-lying, and there have been years of famine. The people's difficulties have not been alleviated. Since the beginning of summer, there has been heavy rain for many days, and flash floods have occurred. The Ying and Huai rivers have risen simultaneously, and the banks have collapsed and the embankments have breached, turning the entire county into a swamp. In Zhao Jiaji, Run Heji, Qiujiadi, Lingtai, and other places along the Huai River, more than 5,000 households of houses have been washed away, and countless people and livestock have been drowned. No less than 20,000 people have no homes to return to. The local Red Swastika Society believes that the disaster situation is severe and that relief is urgently needed. It has appealed to all parties for relief.

▲ Fuyang: Fuyang is the largest county in Anhui Province, and this time the flood was the largest and the disaster was the most severe. When the floodwaters rose sharply, there was torrential rain that did not stop for ten days. The water rose more than thirty feet, with towering waves, unprecedented. The Huai River water surface was hundreds of miles wide in some places, and the city walls were surrounded by water, in extreme danger. The entire territory was a vast expanse of water, with an estimated 50,000 households submerged and more than 2,000 people dead. Residents were scattered and half-submerged in water. Even those who climbed on the roofs of houses and trees had no way to survive and no way to appeal for help. Once they encountered wind and waves, they were swept into the water and became companions with the water gods. All circles in the county believe that the disaster situation is extremely tragic and that the refugees are crying out for food. A disaster relief association has been organized to raise relief funds and appeal to all parties to quickly allocate funds for disaster relief.

▲ Tianchang: Tianchang is located between the Yangtze and Huai rivers, bordering Jiangsu Province, and is the easternmost county in Anhui Province. It borders Gaoyou, Jieshou, and Bao Ying three lakes to the northeast, and the Baita River runs through it. The terrain is low-lying and prone to floods. There were major floods in 1916, 1921, and 1926. At the beginning of this month, there was heavy rain that lasted for several days and nights. The city and the countryside became a swamp. The new and old dike fields were all submerged. The white waves were滔滔, and the water and sky were the same色. The autumn crops in the fields were completely submerged in water, and countless residents' houses collapsed. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented since the beginning of the Republic. The county government has reported the disaster to the provincial government and requested relief.

▲ Xuyi: Xuyi is located in the lower reaches of the Huai River, bordering Hongze Lake to the north. The terrain is low-lying. The southeast is mountainous, and the terrain is relatively high. This time, there was continuous heavy rain, and the Huai River water level rose by thirty feet. The dikes and embankments were breached, and the riverbanks collapsed, resulting in a flood. In the Mingguang Zilaiqiao area in the southeast, flash floods broke out, and the water was even greater. The entire territory was a vast expanse of water, becoming a swamp. The people suffered heavy losses. The county authorities believed that the disaster situation was extremely severe and have telegraphed the province to report the disaster, requesting the allocation of funds for relief to save the survivors.

▲ Huaiyuan: Huaiyuan's terrain is low-lying, shaped like the bottom of a pot. This time, there was heavy rain for many days, flash floods broke out, and the rivers overflowed. The Huai River rose sharply by several dozen feet. The force of the water was unstoppable, causing the city and countryside to become a water kingdom. In addition, the hurricane blew and stirred up huge waves. The Huai Dike breached more than a hundred feet, and the water was滔天, flooding the wilderness, rushing downwards, and the momentum was extremely turbulent. Hundreds of miles of villages, houses, and livestock were almost completely submerged by the floods. Countless people drowned, and the surviving old, young, women, and children were displaced, gathering in the mountains, lying伏穷巖, moaning in the secluded valleys, having no place to栖片帍, and their kitchens were断烟. The Huaiyuan Flood Disaster Relief Association sent a letter to the Bengbu General Chamber of Commerce, appealing for the disaster victims. Sun Yuanfu and other standing committee members of the Chamber of Commerce, due to their hometown relationship, raised 200 bags of rice and transported them to Huaiyuan, which were handed over to the Relief Committee and the County Chamber of Commerce for distribution.

▲ Fengtai: Fengtai is located on the north bank of the Huai River and is the smallest and most impoverished county. This month, the continuous rain caused a disaster, and the water levels of the Huai and Fei rivers rose simultaneously. Many dikes and embankments were washed flat, and the entire territory was a vast expanse of water, becoming a swamp. Only the terrain in the west of the county was higher, and the water was slightly shallower. A person named Cao in the south of the county, seeing the flood rushing in, knew that there was no hope of escape. He tied his entire family of seven, men, women, old, and young, together with a long rope and went into the water to die together. The bodies floated to the Huai River and drifted downstream. A few days ago, they drifted to the river below this place, where they were finally fished out. It was also tragic. Within the disaster area, the crops were gone, and most of the villages were submerged in water. The autumn harvest was completely hopeless.

▲ Huoqiu: Huoqiu is located south of Yingshang, bordering the Huai River, and bordering Liuan and Gushi. The soil in the south of the county is fertile and has always been known as a rich area. In recent years, it has suffered from赤禍, and nine out of ten houses are empty. The north of the county is slightly low-lying due to its proximity to the Huai River. This time, the Huai River breached, and the water was very great. In addition, the East and West Lakes overflowed at the same time. Therefore, the northern border of the county has become a swamp. The crops and houses have been washed away, and countless people and livestock have been drowned. Disaster victims have come in groups to the east to flee the disaster, residing in the old Governor's Office and Guanyue Temple in Bengbu, totaling more than 500 people. The Huoqiu Compatriots Association in Bengbu has telegraphed the Central Disaster Relief Committee, requesting relief funds. The Disaster Relief Committee allocated 1,000 yuan, which was handed over to the Bengbu Public Security Bureau to collect and distribute on its behalf. After the Public Security Bureau received it, it distributed it separately in conjunction with the Huoqiu Compatriots Association Red Swastika Branch. (July 20th)

After Deflan, the Murderer in the Wang Case in Dexian County, Was Escorted to Jinan

▲ The US Consul Repeatedly Demanded Extradition

▲ The Provincial Government Telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for Instructions

Jinan Correspondence: In the case of Deflan, the deputy director of the Weishi Boji Hospital in Dexian County, shooting and killing the Chinese worker Wang Guoqing, the provincial government has telegraphed the Dexian County government, ordering Deflan to be escorted to Jinan yesterday (20th) and temporarily guarded by the Jinan Public Security Bureau. However, US Consul General Mihard has repeatedly demanded extradition. The provincial government, after the abolishment of the Foreign Affairs Office, according to the post-processing measures announced by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, was not convenient to advocate. On the same day, it telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for a detailed reply to base the handling. Today (21st) at about 4:00 PM, the US Consul again went to the provincial government to demand extradition. The provincial government replied that it had telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for instructions and that it could not be extradited temporarily before receiving a reply telegram. Currently, Deflan is in the No. 4 cell of the Jinan Public Security Bureau detention center. He is treated extremely well, and his daily life and diet are all sanitary, but he cannot move freely. The provincial government's telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is as follows: "Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Nanjing, with respect, secret, the case of Deflan, an American at the Boji Hospital in Dexian County, shooting and killing the Chinese worker Wang Guoqing, the deleted telegram should have been received. Later, because the public sentiment in the county was激昂, I was deeply afraid that the case would expand and accidents would occur. According to Article 11 of the Sino-US Treaty, I have ordered the collection of Deflan and escort to the province for transfer to the Jinan Municipal Government for temporary custody. The US Consul stationed in Jinan is currently demanding extradition, but it has not yet been transferred. In addition to the detailed sequel telegram, the matter concerns foreign affairs. According to the post-processing measures of the abolished Foreign Affairs Office of your ministry, the local government does not dare to preside over it. How should this case be handled? Please reply by telegram as soon as possible. Seal of the Shandong Provincial Government." (21st)

Sun Hongzhe of the Jiangsu Construction Department Inspects the Water Situation in Jiangbei

The water level of the canal in Jiangbei, Jiangsu Province, has risen, and it has only recently begun to stabilize slightly. However, it rained again yesterday and the day before, and the area along the canal is still in the period of rushing to protect it. Mao Yisheng, Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, has arrived in Gaoyou to meet with Wu Tongju, Director of the Canal Construction Office. Director Wu returned to Zhenjiang from Gaoyou yesterday to report the situation of the flood to Sun Hongzhe of the Construction Department. According to reports, the canal water level has reached the堤, and the water outlets of the dams returning to the Yangtze River are a vast expanse of water. When will Director Mao return to the bureau? It depends on how the water situation develops in the future. The Construction Department is requesting the Finance Department to quickly allocate funds for the construction and prevention of disasters to meet urgent needs. At the same time, it plans to request the provincial government to send a special commissioner to supervise the construction. Director Sun has also decided to leave for Yangzhou by car across the river at 7:00 AM today (23rd), then take the new spring small wheel to inspect the water situation in the upper and lower reaches of the canal. In addition, according to the telegrams from various places to the Water Conservancy Bureau yesterday, the water level in Bengbu has dropped by 4 meters, with a stored water level of 19.79 meters. The water level in 灣 has increased by 4.6 centimeters, with a stored water level of 18.843 meters. The water level in Gouzha has increased by 4 inches, with a stored water level of 1 zhang and 8 chi and 5 cun. The water level in Gaoyou Yumatou has increased by 2 inches, with a stored water level of 1 zhang and 4 chi and 9 cun. This is due to the impact of the Huai River rising a few days ago. The water level in Bengbu has been falling repeatedly, and the phenomenon has improved slightly. Although the water level in 灣 has risen, the Liu Laojian Dam has been opened and can be discharged into the Liutang River to the sea as much as possible, which may not have much impact on the inner运. (23rd)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Zhang Tongsheng, the Pseudo-Regiment Commander's Confession: The lake bandit formerly belonged to the command of Taibao Ashu, who has been executed. Zhang Tongsheng, the pseudo-regiment commander, also known as Gaojiaopai Siquan, hid in Chang'an Bridge, Wuxi. After Fan, the captain of the Water Police, arrested Miao Aye, who had served in the death squad of the pig's head Amu, he learned the whereabouts of Zhang, led three police ships and captured him. He was once escorted to Jinshanzui Township to find weapons but found nothing. He was taken back to the Zhujing team headquarters for preliminary interrogation. According to the bandit's confession, he followed Taibao Ashu, the pig's head Amu, and others in kidnapping French women in Taihu Lake and robbing various towns in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. He admitted everything. Captain Fan, considering the bandit's serious crimes, ordered strict custody and prepared a document to be sent to the Minhang District Department for transfer to the Command Headquarters for review.

County Party Department Appeals Regarding the Wan Case: The forced farming and digging of ditches by Koreans in Wanbaoshan, infringing upon the sovereignty of tenant farmers, has caused a public outcry. The County Executive Committee of this county has also telegraphed the National Government's Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting serious negotiations and pledging to be a backing.

Suzhou

The New Finance Director Took Office Yesterday Morning: Yuan Xiaogu, Director of the Finance Bureau of Wu County, was approved to resign. The vacancy was filled by Shen Bingzhan, the current Director of the Finance Bureau of Songjiang County. Shen has already handed over his duties at the Finance Bureau of Songjiang County and arrived in Suzhou from Shanghai at 9:00 AM on the 23rd. After getting off the car, he went to the Finance Bureau to take office. The former Director Yuan handled the handover procedures according to the law. It is said that the heads of each section will be changed.

The Farmers' Bank Admitted Trainees: The Suzhou Farmers' Bank recruited trainees on the 19th of this month. On that day, more than 190 people applied for the exam. After the written test, Yang Fengshu, the Deputy General Manager of the Head Office, and Sun Boyan, the Manager of the First District Branch, conducted oral examinations separately. All the test papers were evaluated by Chen, the head of the Preparatory Office of the bank. It is learned that the admitted students are: Wang Xiang, Le Shi, Tao Rong, Cao Zuyin, Xie Mingxia, Yan Jiaxiong, as regular students; Wu Zhaolin, Cao Zhenqun, Pan Xianghe, Yao Erfang, Tao Xiji, Zhou Zonglu, as alternate students. It is said that the bank increased the number of alternate students by two due to the large number of applicants. At the same time, the Zhenjiang First District Branch admitted four female students: Yan Keyu, Liu Xuekun, as regular students; Wang Ruobing, Wang Shenyi, as alternate students.

Kunshan

The Garrisoned Soldiers in Kunshan Seized a Huge Amount of Opium: There are no less than dozens of well-known opium dealers in Kunshan. The organization meets at a certain tea house on Zhengyang Bridge. These people are very agile, making it impossible for the government to arrest them. The opium dealer Zhang Laowu, due to a dispute with a fellow dealer, reported to Hu Chengzhu, the squad leader of the Garrisoned Soldiers in Kunshan, and the soldier Sun Liren, saying that a certain train arriving in Kunshan had a large batch of opium unloaded. He requested an immediate arrest. Upon receiving the report, Hu went to wait beside Waiyangqi. When the train was about to arrive, he saw a large package of opium (300 taels) thrown from the train. A certain opium dealer stepped forward to pick it up. At that time, squad leader Hu ordered him to put it down and took the opium away. Afterwards, Zhang Laowu managed to recover the seized opium completely. The matter was learned by Battalion Commander Wen of the battalion. He immediately summoned squad leader Hu Chengzhu and soldier Sun Liren and arrested Zhang Laowu and the well-known opium dealer Run Zongren. After questioning, on the 23rd, he prepared a document to submit all the persons to the First Regiment Headquarters in Wuxi for disposal.

Wuxi

The Hidden Reefs of the Cigarette Industry and Tobacco Shops: The county has added new urban areas and its population has increased year by year, and the cigarette industry has also developed accordingly. Originally, there was a cigarette paper industry association formed by cigarette paper dealers. Besides the incense cigarette companies stationed in Wuxi, all industries are now reorganizing into trade associations. The cigarette industry has also recently reorganized according to law. More than a dozen companies engaged in the wholesale of incense cigarettes, such as Da Mei, Zhou Yuansheng, Fu Taiyuan, Feng Taiyuan, and Tai Kang, initiated the reorganization to form the Cigarette Trade Association. However, there are a total of six or seven hundred tobacco shops, large and small, in the city. Previously, they all belonged to one association, but now they have been abandoned by the major firms and are resentful. They are also secretly initiating the organization of a tobacco shop trade association. The name is compliant and does not violate laws and regulations. The major firms learned of this and immediately tried to win over some tobacco shops to join their association in order to divide the organization. However, the number of tobacco shops is still not small, and they are now actively organizing according to the precedents in Shanghai and other places, and will soon be able to announce their establishment.

Continuous Rainstorms and Expanding Disaster: After two heavy rains this month, the river water in the county rose sharply, and low-lying fields have become a watery world. Fortunately, the river water gradually receded, and the disaster did not expand. Who knew that on the night of the twenty-second, the weather was unusually cool, the thermometer reached seventy-two degrees, the heavy rain continued, and the river water suddenly rose. The water volume has exceeded the highest level of the previous time, and even slightly higher low-lying fields are in imminent danger. The disaster is expanding and cannot be contained. Houses in low-lying areas in urban and rural areas have been submerged in water, and many have collapsed. Fields, gardens, and vegetables have been submerged in water, and prices are surprisingly high. There are no vegetables to be found in the low-lying areas.

The Chamber of Commerce's Position on Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese: All Chinese people are deeply indignant about the Korean Wanbaoshan case. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has initiated the organization of an All-Circles Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese Committee, and has resolved four measures. The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce has also telegraphed the central government to clearly define its diplomatic policy in order to concentrate efforts, and advised all industries related to Japanese goods to pay attention to the measures set by Shanghai and wait for the county party headquarters to lead the handling. Furthermore, since the central government is now actively suppressing the communists, and there have been many rumors in the north recently that the Japanese are using traitors to engage in sabotage, as evidenced by the Wanbaoshan case, which is a customary trick, there are many deep concerns in our country. Within the scope of not harming the country's economy and not hindering social public order, we should follow the central government's leadership and actively participate. As for Japanese goods in the interior of Jiangsu Province, they are all imported from Shanghai. If Shanghai can investigate, detain, and completely eliminate them, there will be no problem in the interior. Yesterday, a special telegram was sent to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to lead and actively proceed to prevent Japanese goods from being transported in, which would protect the commerce in the interior. At the same time, separate telegrams were sent to the Central National Government, the Jiangsu Provincial Party Department, and the Provincial Government to request instructions on policy for consistency. On the one hand, various industries were also encouraged to actively raise funds and remit them to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce for transfer to aid overseas Chinese.

The Rising Water Level at Lujiangkou and Defense: The 14th Branch of the Public Security Bureau, considering that Lujiangkou in its jurisdiction is an important route to enter the lake, previously consulted with the 17th District Office and resolved to set up water gates at the entrance of the river to prohibit ships from traveling to prevent lake bandits from infiltrating. Who knew that recently, due to continuous heavy rains, the lake water rose sharply, the wooden piles sank, and were entangled by aquatic plants, blocking the water flow, resulting in the submergence of more than a thousand acres of rice seedlings nearby. After discussion, it was decided to remove the wooden piles, but once removed, the defense would inevitably be empty. Yesterday, a special report was submitted to the Public Security Bureau for forwarding to County Chief Chen, requesting the dispatch of four patrol boats to be stationed permanently, so that water conservancy and defense can be taken care of at the same time, and banditry can be prevented.

Changzhou

Liu Hongzhao Handed Over Public Funds in Full During His Term: Liu Hongzhao, the former director of the Finance Bureau of the county, rushed to complete the handover immediately after leaving office. Yesterday, he specially invited party and government agencies and local gentry to conduct a public review. In addition to the fact that special funds had been fully allocated, not only was there no hidden deposit under the provincial tax items, but also seven thousand yuan of loans had been cleared.

Zhenjiang

Another Rural Case in Gaozi Township, West of the County: Gaozi Township in the west of the county has been plagued by bandits year after year, with looting, extortion, arson, and killings, and there has been no peace. Fortunately, the 4th Battalion of the 3rd Infantry Regiment of the Security Force searched and suppressed the bandits in the town for several months, and the bandits began to disappear. Now, because they are stationed in Xiashu, the bandits have become rampant again. The other night, dozens of bandits suddenly took away Xiao Bangkui and Xiao Longfu in Xiaojiazhuang. Yesterday, one person was taken away in Zhuke Village in the mountains. Now the head of the Second District, Tong Jiasheng, has sent people to investigate and telegraphed the county government on his behalf to forward the report to the Security Office, requesting the dispatch of a team to station there as soon as possible to deter the bandits.

Speculative Merchants Import Japanese Goods on a Large Scale: Since the Wanbaoshan massacre occurred, people everywhere have been indignant. Zhenjiang, as an important trading port in Jiangbei, has seen that the Zhenjiang Party Department has organized a Support Association for Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese and will implement a boycott of Japanese goods. General unscrupulous merchants are now seeing that the Zhenjiang Party Department has organized the Anti-Japanese Aid to Overseas Chinese Support Association and will implement a boycott of Japanese goods. They are deeply afraid of affecting their business, so recently, sugar merchants in the Yaoyiguan area have been particularly panicked, with cars and porters transporting goods all day long. Even if they don't have time to unload goods during the day, they continue to do so at night. Even though it has been raining these past few days, they have not stopped. Other industries have also purchased goods in large quantities.

Yao Mingrang Released on Bail: Yao Mingrang, the former director of the Jingjiang Construction Bureau, was dismissed for embezzling public funds, and the Construction Department investigated and handed him over to the Zhenjiang Court for investigation. He was taken into custody. After being detained, Yao filed a petition for bail, which was approved. Yesterday, he was notified to present one thousand yuan of public bonds to offset three thousand yuan of bail to the court, and was immediately released to await summons.

Yangzhou

Huang Yunxuan Throws Himself into the Net Again: Huang Yunxuan of Xiaoliufang Lane in this city, two months ago, represented his relative Tang Lin and Chen Hongfu in filing a complaint with the Superintendent's Office due to a real estate dispute. He was rejected and ignored. Later, Chen accused Huang of impersonating a military officer of the Superintendent's Office to extort money. The Superintendent's Office summoned Huang and Chen for interrogation, and it was found that Huang Yunxuan was not suspected of impersonating a military officer, and Chen Hongfu was making a false accusation out of malice. Huang was released, and an official document was prepared to transfer Chen to the Procuratorate of the Jiangdu County Court for custody, investigation, and handling. After repeated investigations and inquiries by the Procuratorate, the investigation was concluded and a decision was made not to prosecute, and Chen was released. However, Huang Yunxuan was still unwilling and accused Chen at the Superintendent's Office, believing that the allegations were contradictory and abnormal. The Superintendent's Office again took Huang into custody at the Public Security Bureau to await investigation.

Prison Warden Arrested for Smoking Opium: Cao Yukun, a prison warden in Jiangdu County, was accused of smoking opium and reported to the High Court, which secretly ordered the Jiangdu County Court to conduct a thorough investigation and report back. It is reported that after receiving the order, the court sent personnel to investigate the prison warden and confirmed that he had a habit. This morning (22nd) at 7:00 a.m., Judge Huang Zhe and Clerk Yin Yongxi were dispatched to search for evidence in the prison warden's bedroom, and they found smoking paraphernalia and opium dregs. Judge Huang immediately brought the prison warden and the paraphernalia to the court for interrogation. The warden admitted to smoking opium. President Chen believed that the prison warden was under the jurisdiction of the county government, so he transferred him to the county government for custody. At the same time, the court reported to the High Court for instructions on how to handle the case.

Continued Investigation of the Qianjiashan Massacre: It is reported that in the case of burying people alive in Qianjiashan, in the west of the county, the murderer Qian Sanxi's son Xue Youfu and Da Hualian, because the authorities had news of the investigation, secretly dug out the body from the pit in the middle of the night, put it in a coffin, and gathered the villagers nearby to sign a circular document, aiming to eliminate the distinction between principal offenders and accomplices, falsely claiming public opinion, and many mourned the innocent dead and refused to sign. The outcome is unknown.

Nantong

Remedies for Local Financial Difficulties: The local finances of Nantong have recently been extremely strained.

The Property Office issued 30,000 yuan of temporary loan certificates and borrowed 35,000 yuan from industrial and financial circles to pay for accumulated political, police, and self-government expenses. The county government stated that the county's provincial tax revenue is 100,000 yuan per year, but the advances often exceed more than double that amount, so it submitted a report to the provincial government for forwarding to the department, requesting that notifications be issued within the scope of provincial tax revenue. Furthermore, considering that the supplementary tax on salt land differs greatly from that on civilian land, it was decided to convene a meeting of salt land field managers, district chiefs, and representatives of various agencies on August 2 to discuss the average burden method for civilians and salt workers.

Education Bureau Takes Over All Confucius Temples in the County: The Education Bureau, upon receiving instructions from the department, will jointly with the county take over the Confucius temples in various districts of the county, as well as all assets and equipment, to expand education.

Jiangbei Automobile Industry Opposes Revising New Regulations: The automobile industry in various counties in Jiangbei opposed the revision of the new automobile donation regulations by the Construction Department and went on strike to oppose the donation. The Nantong Construction Bureau has telegraphed the department to postpone the implementation.

Rugao

The Trend of Draining Water from Juegang is Increasing Day by Day: The tail end of the Jianxiaoshuai Changhe River in Juegang City of this county, which is also the junction point of the upper end of the public river, is separated by an earth dam with a water hole, called the Dragon King Cave. The drainage of the waterway outside the dam all depends on this cave. However, due to the terrain, the water from Chenjiayuan and various ponds in the northwest exits from this cave, and the effect is very weak. Recently, heavy rains have caused disasters, and the rice fields have been flooded, so the earth dam was opened to connect with the salt land public river to facilitate drainage and allow the water to enter the sea. However, because the salt residents outside the dam have low-lying terrain, the rice seedlings have been submerged. The route for drainage has been obstructed by the dikes built by various salt reclamation companies, and it is about to become a watery world. If the water from the dikes is poured in again, it will be like adding fuel to the fire, which is unthinkable. Therefore, the salt residents of the sixth, seventh, eighth, and ninth districts went to the district office and various agencies on the 15th to petition, demanding to build up the earth dam, but there was no result. The salt residents then automatically built it up. On the 16th, the farmers from the dike farmland gathered more than a hundred people and opened the dam again. Who knew that while they were working, the salt farmers gathered three or four hundred people with gongs and drums, each carrying agricultural implements. The farmers from the dike farmland saw the situation was not good and fled. The dam was still blocked by the salt residents. Farmers from both the farmland and salt land have disputes over water drainage due to their respective interests, as described above. The drainage of water from the salt land is almost entirely controlled by the Da Yu Company and various warehouses, disregarding the lives of the Lao圩 farmers. Previously, because the gates and dams were closed, many tenant farmers were beaten and injured. On the 16th, the village chiefs and deputy chiefs of various salt land villages invited people from all walks of life to hold a meeting in Zhongshan Hall to discuss solutions. They unanimously resolved to submit a petition to the county government to quickly investigate the situation and provide relief, open the Lujia River, and order the companies to open various dams and gates to facilitate drainage, and to punish the murderers of the dead and injured. While the meeting was in progress, farmers from both the farmland and salt land came to petition. The resolved solutions were announced to the public, and then they dispersed. The merchants and residents of the city also believed that the Da Yu Company prohibited the salt residents from draining water and arbitrarily beat and killed people, so they went on strike from the 16th to support them, and the market has not yet opened until today (20th). The outcome of this matter is unknown.

Hangzhou

Two嵊 County Bandits Executed by Firing Squad: The notorious bandit Liu Baocheng (alias Dong Qianjia Die) from 嵊 County repeatedly colluded with bandits such as Zhang Hanquan and Zhang Shiming, using guns to kidnap Jin Baixiang and others and demanding ransom, committing many crimes. Zhang Chunhe, the captain of the 10th team of the county's militia patrol, led his team to suppress the bandits in the Xiangnan District and captured the notorious bandit at the foot of Badouguling. In addition, the 嵊 County bandit Yao Linlao had repeatedly kidnapped five or six "Gods of Wealth." The other day, he sneaked back to his home in Jinxi and was detected by the 2nd company of the 1st battalion of the 6th Security Regiment, who rushed to capture him. Both confessed during interrogation and were sentenced to death. The sentences have been submitted to the provincial government for approval and were executed by firing squad immediately.

Murderer's Appeal Rejected, Death Sentence Upheld: You Mingzhai, a 24-year-old farmer from Linhai, was previously accused of committing a serious murder case in his hometown. After a trial by the local court, the facts of the case were clarified and he was sentenced to death. You filed an appeal and was sent to Hangzhou in January and detained in the High Court's detention center. After several trials, the case has been concluded. Yesterday, the First Criminal Division of the High Court announced its verdict, upholding the original sentence and ordering him to be sent back to his hometown in Linhai for execution.

Another Suspect Arrested in the Longjing Kidnapping and Murder Case: The Cantonese merchant Li Jiyun was kidnapped by bandits at Longjing in West Lake and brutally murdered at Songhe Villa. The criminals Wang Yang, Wang E, Wu Jingyuan, Ying Aying, etc., have been sentenced to death and life imprisonment respectively. Subsequently, Wang Shizhen, the principal offender in the case, was captured and brought back to the court. It is now reported that the detective team of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau has arrested another suspect, Shi Dafu, in Hengxi, Yuhang. It is said that Shi is a clerk in a rice shop in Maojiabu, West Lake. Li used to disembark at the door of the shop every morning. Afterwards, Shi suddenly fled, so he is highly suspected. After being interrogated by the court, he was ordered to be detained.

Shangyu

The 6th Regiment Stationed in Baiguan Dispatches Troops to Suppress Bandits: Sun Libiao's bandit gang from Fenghua has repeatedly committed acts of rape, looting, arson, and murder in places such as Da'ao, Yuanjia, Aosunjia, and Shimen in the county, and the local area has been severely ravaged. County Chief Zhang of the county telegraphed the Provincial Security Office and the 6th Security Regiment stationed in Baiguan for help. It is now reported that Wu Conglong, the commander of the regiment, specially ordered Zhang Jiling, an adjunct of the regiment, to lead Zhuang Youxin, the battalion commander of the 2nd battalion of the regiment, and soldiers of the 6th company to assist.

Dong Shuchen Accused of Embezzling Relief Funds: Wang Chunfu, a citizen of Dongjiashan in the west of the county, recently accused Dong Shuchen, a wealthy household in the area, to the county party headquarters of embezzling a large amount of relief funds for the Wangxu water disaster, requesting that the case be forwarded to the provincial party headquarters for thorough investigation.

The Qixiang Bureau Arrests Unemployed Vagrants: The Shaoxing Qixiang Bureau, upon receiving orders, arrested unemployed vagrants. The Public Security Bureau ordered various urban and rural sub-bureaus to go out and arrest them, and more than fifty people have been sent to the city in recent days.
