Mingguang

The Tragic Situation of Flooding in Various Counties in Eastern Anhui: There has been torrential rain in eastern Anhui for the entire month, and rivers have overflowed, causing a major disaster. The disaster situation in various counties is recorded below. The eastern border of Dingyuan is the source of the Chi River. On the 5th of this month, there was torrential rain. On the 6th, the torrents from the Wanghuigang mountains rushed down, and the water level was as high as ten feet. As a result, the entire Chi River bank became a watery world, and the towns of Daiqiao, Outang, Renhe, and Sanhe were all several feet deep in water. Countless villages were submerged, and more than a thousand people died. It was truly a catastrophe. The northwest township of Lingbi, which borders the Chi River, was also severely affected. All the most productive agricultural areas of Hongmiao, Jiaocheng, Chendui, Qili, and Jiansi, etc., were submerged, and there is no hope for the autumn harvest. Wuhe is the confluence of several rivers. This time, all the rivers overflowed, and the torrents from Sanhejian, Zhengyangguan, and other places rushed straight down. On the 7th, dozens of sections of the western embankment of the Huai River collapsed, and the water level is now more than ten feet above the embankment. The entire county has suffered a major flood. Except for a section of North Main Street, the entire town is a vast expanse of water. The extent of the disaster can be imagined. Fearing that the roadbed would be destroyed by the water, the railway authorities transported a large amount of gravel on the 19th to reinforce the roadbed. The small ferries of Wudang and Wuling suspended operations one after another due to the excessive water level. The floodwaters in Mingguang have receded very slowly, and the disaster area is still a vast expanse of water. The victims are scattered in the Houshantou area, exposed to the wind and dew, and their situation is extremely tragic. Recently, there have been continuous heavy rains, and the water has risen again. Alas, the people of this place have nowhere to die.

Letter

Letter from the General Distribution Office of Huachang Factory Sanitary Paint:

To the editor, Regarding the news published in your newspaper on the 18th of this month, stating that the Hangzhou Civil Affairs Department seized three hundred cans and one large box of opium substitutes from the Hangzhou branch of the Shanghai Huachang Manufacturing Factory, after investigation, the sanitary paint produced by our factory is made by using crushed leather to compound and chemicalize medicinal liquids, and has been tested by the Central Sanitation Experiment Institute and the Customs Experiment Office to be non-toxic, and has been given certificates, and has been approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the National Registration Bureau, and various provincial official offices for protection. It is used to paint utensils, making them bright, durable, and odorless. Since its launch, it has been famous far and wide. This time, the Hangzhou Civil Affairs Department was misreported, resulting in the search of our products. In addition to sending letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and other organizations to request the Zhejiang Provincial authorities to thoroughly investigate and clear our name, the Hangzhou Civil Affairs Department sent personnel to the Huasheng Road Manufacturing Factory on the 18th to investigate the results in conjunction with Chinese and Western detectives from the Public Concession Patrol Room. No prohibited items were found. The Western detectives stated on the spot that the factory has been operating for many years, manufacturing oils, and does not contain any opium toxins, and the Concession authorities have approved its operation. The truth of this matter will be revealed soon. Fearing that false rumors may hinder our factory's reputation and business, we have described the situation and ask your newspaper to correct it. Sincerely, Shanghai Huachang Factory

Educational News

Important News

Ministry of Education Orders That Normal School Students Must Serve for One Year Before Being Allowed to Enter University

The Ministry of Education has issued an order to the education departments of various provinces and cities, national universities, and vocational schools that graduates of high school normal departments who have received free treatment must serve for one year before being allowed to enter university. It is stated that the method for normal school graduates of senior high schools to enter university has been instructed by the Ministry to National Zhejiang University and published in the Gazette. The high school normal department was originally established to train primary school teachers or other personnel serving in the education field. Students receive free treatment during their studies and should have service obligations after graduation. These students should be slightly restricted from applying to vocational schools and above. Therefore, the previous order is reiterated to clearly stipulate that all graduates mentioned above, whether they are exempted from all or part of their tuition, food, lodging fees, must have proof of service in the education field for more than one year before they can apply to public or registered private vocational schools and above. In addition to distributing the instructions, this order is hereby issued to the department for forwarding to the provincial and registered private vocational schools and above for compliance, and to instruct all public senior high schools to be informed of this order.

Ministry of Education's Instructions on University Admission for Rural Teachers

The Ministry of Education also received a report from Huang Jiabai stating that since the level of students graduating from rural teacher special programs is equivalent to that of those who have completed the second grade of senior high school normal departments, can they be inserted into the third grade of senior high school according to the old system of university admission for normal school graduates? Are there any restrictions on the departments they can enter? The Ministry of Education instructed that since the graduation level of rural teacher special programs is equivalent to the second grade of senior high school normal departments, those who wish to continue their studies can be handled according to the old system of senior high school enrollment for normal school graduates stipulated in the Ministry's Instruction No. 976 of the previous year, but they must be limited to applying for senior high school normal departments or normal schools. The admission standards should still be subject to the strict examination of the school in order to ensure the connection of levels. Please be informed accordingly.

Investigator Xu of the Jiangsu Education Department Destroys Education in Songjiang: An Appeal

To the Fellow Villagers of Songjiang in Shanghai:

We, Xu Pengzu and 575 other teachers and staff of primary and secondary schools in Songjiang, respectfully address you, esteemed gentlemen of Songjiang residing in Shanghai. The education budget for Songjiang, since the 17th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1928], has been allocated according to the minimum standards stipulated by Zhongshan University. By the 19th year [1930] budget, it had already been drastically reduced by the Education Department, causing actual difficulties. However, due to strict official decrees, we have endured the hardship until now. With the 20th year [1931] budget, it was further reduced by the Education Department. School administrators were already deeply concerned. Unexpectedly, Xu Xihuang, a staff member from the Education Department, came to Songjiang for investigation and suddenly drastically reduced the already approved 20th-year budget, amounting to over 37,000 yuan, reaching three-tenths of the total education expenses of the entire county. Furthermore, based on his personal negative views, he ordered the closure of more than 30 schools. Such destruction of education and mistreatment of teachers is a clear violation of the late Premier's exhortation to revitalize education and disregards the National Assembly's motion to improve treatment. Such retrograde actions have gone too far. Upon investigation, Songjiang education funds have savings and have never been in deficit. Even the newly added land tax has been kept untouched, as instructed. However, Investigator Xu acted according to his own whims, falsely reporting to the Education Department and forcing schools to stop operating, like "abandoning eating for fear of choking" and "cutting the feet to fit the shoes." The sudden shock has left us in a state of panic and bewilderment. In addition to sending telegrams to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Ministry of Education, the Provincial Party Headquarters, and the Provincial Government requesting correction, we also earnestly implore you, gentlemen, to provide assistance in your esteemed newspaper to safeguard the education of our hometown and benefit its progress. We would be immensely grateful.

Respectfully,

Xu Pengzu, Wang Chengxun, Chen Guisan, Shen Fusun, Zhu Zhu, and 575 other teachers and staff of primary and secondary schools in Songjiang County.

Attached: Facts of the Matter

Upon investigation, although Songjiang's education budget is not affluent, it is sufficient to maintain operations. Since the 17th year, school expenses have been allocated according to the minimum standards stipulated by Zhongshan University, leaving no cause for concern about inadequacy. Therefore, in past years, there have been no unfortunate incidents such as arrears in school expenses or unpaid salaries for teachers and staff. The Education Bureau's budget submissions have not indicated any shortfall or requested guidance on solutions. This proves that Songjiang's education funds can maintain the current state. Why should it be exhausted or bankrupted? However, Xu Xihuang, the investigator appointed by the Education Department, hastily conducted a brief inquiry, disregarding the truth, and abruptly claimed that this year's budget required a deficit of 111,000 yuan. If Investigator Xu's words are true, why didn't the Education Bureau consider this when submitting the 20th-year budget? Why did the Education Department approve it after review? It is clearly evident that Investigator Xu's investigation was negligent and did not align with the facts. The resulting impact is that primary and secondary schools are unable to maintain operations due to arbitrary budget cuts, causing a sudden drastic change to the stable educational state in Songjiang. Can it be said that Investigator Xu did not intend to destroy it? Our late Premier's views on revitalizing and expanding education are found in his doctrines and speeches. Yet Investigator Xu is destroying and undermining it. How can such words and actions come from an educational administrator under the Three Principles of the People? Furthermore, the inaccuracies in Investigator Xu's report and plan are self-evident. For example, when reducing primary and secondary school expenses, he merely stated a certain amount was reduced in general terms, without specifying which item was reduced by how much. This shows that he did not carefully examine the facts and based it solely on speculation. Such important education expenses can be arbitrarily allocated, revealing the extent of the errors. According to the 17th-year budget for primary school senior grades, with four classrooms in the senior level, the annual amount was 5,496 yuan. In the 19th-year budget, with four classrooms in the senior level, the annual amount was 4,476 yuan for Category A and 4,224 yuan for Category B, a reduction of 1,020 yuan to 1,272 yuan. The submitted and approved 20th-year budget allocated 4,140 yuan for Category A and 3,912 yuan for Category B for four classrooms in the senior level, a decrease of 336 yuan and 312 yuan compared to the 19th year, and a decrease of 1,356 yuan to 1,584 yuan compared to the 17th year. The junior levels were also reduced accordingly. Recently, the Department issued an order to suddenly change the already approved 20th-year budget. According to Investigator Xu's plan, each senior level grade would be reduced by another 400 yuan, leaving only 700 yuan. After paying teacher salaries, there would be nothing left for other staff salaries and miscellaneous expenses. It is incomprehensible what standards Investigator Xu used to determine this plan. Primary school tuition revenue is extremely low, even to the point of being non-existent, and books and supplies must be provided free of charge. Now, Investigator Xu calculates that each classroom in urban areas should have 40 students, and rural areas should have 80% of that amount, which is difficult to achieve in reality. In addition, each grade has its recurring expenses reduced by 40 yuan. Whether it can be maintained or not is obvious to those who are perceptive. Our Songjiang secondary schools only have the Provincial Middle School, County Middle School, County Normal School, and County Women's Normal School. The Provincial Middle School also admits out-of-province students. The County Normal School will only recruit junior high school graduates from now on, and the Women's Normal School does not recruit public classes every year. However, the number of elementary school senior level graduates in the current year is over 400, and it is already difficult to accommodate all of them. Yet, Investigator Xu only knows how to save money and does not allow the County Middle School to establish double tracks in the first year, as per the existing plan, but only allows the recruitment of 50 new students. He also does not allow the County Normal School to recruit first-year students, intending to make so many eager students lose their opportunity to study. The intention behind this is difficult to understand. The County Middle School has over 50 students in the second year. According to the regulations, it should be allowed to establish double classes. During Investigator Xu's investigation, the actual attendance was 54 students. However, Investigator Xu incorrectly stated that the actual attendance was only 49 students, and that the 20th year should be combined into one classroom. This is a significant oversight. The County Middle School originally had two instructors, as it was more convenient and effective to train male and female students separately. However, Investigator Xu did not understand this point and planned to cut one person. Examining the facts, there is no agreement on the top. Although the County Normal School's school buildings are not spacious, adding a grade is more than sufficient. Although the facilities are not perfect, they are gradually being improved each year. For the sake of implementing teacher training and providing students with a path, it is best to recruit elementary school graduates. However, Investigator Xu insisted on recruiting junior high school graduates, disregarding teacher training and local needs to such an extent. The Women's Normal School, due to limited funding, only pays half the salaries of other secondary schools, paying 50 cents per hour. Therefore, many hired teachers have to take on multiple roles. However, the Women's Normal School, with its limited funding, has established private classes in addition to public classes to remedy the shortage of teachers. Graduates from previous classes who serve in schools have achieved excellent results. However, Investigator Xu only saw that there were fewer full-time teachers and immediately made harsh accusations. It is unlikely that someone with a clear mind would do this. Investigator Xu said that Songjiang is close to Shanghai, but the salaries of teachers and staff are lower than in Shanghai. Therefore, those with better qualifications and more experience flock to Shanghai. This is indeed the reality. With such large-scale budget cuts, the salaries of teachers will certainly be further reduced. Is this not a signal to those seeking improvements to leave quickly? Investigator Xu said that many collection agencies in Songjiang are behind on tax collections, such as having funds from one year being settled two or three years later, causing the revenues and expenditures of education funds to be mismatched. However, it is not known that although the funds from Year C are collected in Years D and E, the funds from Years A and B can be collected in Year C. The funds from Years A and B are used to offset the deficit of Year C, and so on, so there is no shortage. It is only cleared one year at a time.

It only seems like there is a deficit. Investigator Xu said that there is a lot of waste in the school expenses, and they must be greatly reduced. However, the salaries paid to teachers and combatants in each school are in accordance with the regulations, and other expenses are supported by vouchers. Moreover, recurring revenues and expenditures are listed monthly and sent to the Economic Audit Committee for auditing. Even the annual budget was approved by the order. What does the so-called waste mean? In short, Investigator Xu disregarded the facts and arbitrarily reduced the expenses of primary and secondary schools. His statements are often unfair. Whether he had preconceived notions before the investigation, or whether he was not careful during the investigation, we dare not rashly conclude. However, the investigation is untrue, obscuring the authorities, and the plan is inappropriate, affecting education. The blame for dereliction of duty cannot be shirked. Strictly speaking, using a report to destroy the education of primary and secondary schools in our Songjiang and put it in a desperate situation is a major responsibility. Since Investigator Xu said that the reason for the deficit in Songjiang's education expenses lies in the clerks and so on manipulating the funds, the solution should be designed from the tax collection side. However, he did not think about the root cause and only reduced the expenses of the schools. If the clerks manipulate the funds and the education expenses are completely cut off, will Investigator Xu also advocate that our schools in Songjiang be completely closed? How can such retrograde actions go so far? For the sake of the future of education in Songjiang, Pengzu and others convened a joint meeting of primary and secondary school teachers and staff on the 14th of this month to discuss this matter. Everyone agreed to send telegrams to various agencies requesting correction, maintain the original budget of the 17th year, avoid reductions, and maintain education and promote progress.

Local News

Detailed Account of the Compilation of Secondary School Curriculum Standards

The meeting of the secondary school group of the Primary and Secondary School Curriculum Committee on the 22nd, both in the morning and afternoon, has been reported in yesterday's special dispatch in this newspaper. The details are recorded below. Those present on that day were Ren Mengxian, Yao Wencai, Zheng Hesheng, Zhong Daochang, Xu Zhunqi, Dai Yingguan, Xu Yiqiao, Gu Shusen, Wu Yan Yin, Lin Duanfu, Xia Chengfeng, Zhang Guoren, Zhao Naichuan, Zhang Xinfu, Zhu Baoqin, Zhang Shiyi. Weng Zhida was present as an observer, Gu Shusen was the chairman, and Weng Zhida was the recorder. After the chairman reported the resolutions of the previous meeting, the discussion on the general review opinions of various subjects in junior and senior high schools continued. (1) Labor: The industrial arts in junior high school are revised as follows: The objectives are changed to (A) Understanding the relationship between work and life, and developing a concept of equality among all professions; (B) Developing good habits such as diligence, hard work, and precision, and providing the necessary industrial arts for daily life; (C) Preparing a foundation for career or work. The phrase "Ability to understand that doing work is also the duty of students" in the fourth item of the minimum graduation requirement is deleted. A footnote should be added to this standard: "When metalworking and woodworking courses cannot be offered at the same time, at least one course must be offered." The rest is passed according to the general review opinions. (2) Party Principles: Regarding the inclusion of various civic education materials in the Party Principles curriculum in secondary schools, the points originally proposed by the committee appointed by the previous meeting are passed and submitted to the Party Principles Curriculum Review Committee designated by the Central Standing Committee for reference when reviewing the Party Principles curriculum standards. (3) Junior High School History Textbook Outline: Except for medieval history, social and economic materials should be added. The rest is passed in accordance with the revised opinions of Committee Member Zheng and others. (4) Physical Education: For the junior high school physical education curriculum, (A) Objective (6), the phrase "Develop habits of physical fitness and recreation" from the original proposed provisional standard is still used; (B) The terms martial arts and national arts are uniformly referred to as national arts; (C) Distribution of teaching materials, (E) is changed to "National arts unarmed and with weapons must be appropriately distributed"; (D) Minimum graduation requirement item (7) is changed to "Proficient in three or more sets of national arts." The rest is passed in accordance with the review opinions. For senior high school general physical education, (A) Objectives 7 and 8 are changed to a good foundation for specialized physical education, and Objective 8 is deleted; (B) (Teaching time, Group D is changed to "National arts including boxing, kicking, holding, and weapons"; (C) Teaching method point 8 is changed to "The environment for physical education teaching must be conducive to health, and it should contribute to health in all aspects"; (D) Minimum graduation requirement seven is proposed to be changed to proficient in six or more sets of national arts (including unarmed and weapons). The rest is passed in accordance with the review opinions. (5) Music: The opinion letter proposed by Mr. Wang Lianggong is sent to Committee Member Xiao Youmei for reference when revising the provisional music standards. (6) The rest of the subjects still adopt the original proposed provisional standards. (7) Senior High School General Elective Subjects: (A) General Explanation of Senior High School Elective Subjects, 1. According to the original plan, 2. "The third group is for those preparing to enter employment" is deleted, 5. Full study is deleted, 6. is changed to 5, "Elective courses must have at least 15 students to open a class. If a single class has fewer than 40 students, an elective class can also be opened with at least 10 students," 7. is changed to 6, and a seventh item is added: "In the third academic year, senior high schools may establish vocational elective subjects for students who cannot go to college." (B) First Group of Elective Subjects, 1. Outline of Historical Studies is deleted, History of Chinese Literature six credits is added, Outline of English Literature History is deleted, A course in Japanese six credits is added, English Applied Documents three credits is added, Ethics is deleted, An introductory course in Philosophy is added three credits, "and conversation" is added after English Phonetics, one credit is added, 2. Regarding Academic Writing and Outline of Chinese Language, it is decided to decide after investigating the contents of each subject, 3. The rest is passed in accordance with the opinions proposed by the group committee. (C) Second Group of Elective Subjects, 1. The following subjects should be added: Advanced Physics ten credits, Advanced Chemistry six credits, Organic Chemistry three credits, Mechanical Book two credits, Algebra three credits, 2. Analytical Geometry is changed to four to six credits, Arc Trigonometry is changed to Trigonometry (Plane and Spherical), Psychology is deleted, 3. Outline of Calculus, Outline of Astronomy, Outline of Industrial Chemistry, and Outline of Mechanics should all be changed to Preliminary, Outline is deleted after Mineralogy, 4. The rest is passed in accordance with the opinions proposed by the group committee. (D) Reconsideration of the third group of elective subjects, without setting two-thirds, the resolution is passed. (8) Dai Yingguan, Wu Yan Yin, and Zhao Ting are designated to be responsible for reviewing the senior high school history curriculum standards. (9) Temporary Motions: It is resolved that (A) After the Ministry of Education formally publishes the primary and secondary school curriculum standards, all universities should be ordered to base the entrance examination questions on the said curriculum standards; (B) The Ministry of Education should be requested to order all universities and education departments in provinces and cities to pay attention to the training of primary and secondary school teachers based on the primary and secondary school curriculum standards.

Regarding the situation of party-established public schools in this city:

▲ A total of eleven schools have been established.

▲ A total of ten schools are being prepared.

(Guomin News Agency) The public schools established by the various levels of party headquarters under the Shanghai Special Municipality Party Headquarters, the official established one includes the first, third, fourth, and fifth district party headquarters, and the sixth district third, fourth, eighth, and third district branches a total of seven schools. Those still in preparation include the sixth district party headquarters, and the sixth district first, sixth, ninth, tenth, twelfth, (ordered to be办）twelfth, twenty-third, and thirty-fourth district branches, a total of eight schools. The details have been recorded in previous newspapers. Now, in addition to the aforementioned fifteen schools, there are four officially established schools and two schools in preparation that have been reported to the Municipal Training Department. Huizhong Middle School, a Church School, Proceeds with Registration

▲ Western Principal Crawford Resigns… Zhang Dongmin Succeeds

Huizhong Middle School, located at Ximen Xieqiao in this city, has been run by the American Seventh-day Baptist Mission for over 40 years. It has long been known for its reputation in the Christian education community in East China. In the past two or three years, in order to adapt to the new trends, the school has held many meetings to discuss the issue of school registration and seek to proceed with it. However, it was ultimately unable to become a reality because it did not obtain the approval of the American Mission. Until mid-May of this year, after the school's entire faculty and staff finally requested the American Mission, it agreed. Therefore, in the past two months, the school has been proceeding with registration matters. It is now reported that the board of directors has been established and invited thirteen people, including Liu Zhanen, Liao Shicheng, Rong Qizhao, Wang Xinzhai, Zhu Kaichou, Pei Dike, and Sun Henian, to serve as directors. The original Western principal, Mr. Crawford, has also voluntarily resigned, and Zhang Dongmin, Director of the Biology Department of Guanghua University, has been appointed as the new principal. It is also reported that the school's operating policy in the future, in addition to maintaining the original principle of emphasizing quality over quantity, will appropriately balance the number of students due to the completion of the new school building, and add a business department in the senior high school.

Preparation for Modern Middle School

People in Shanghai who are enthusiastic about education have initiated the establishment of a Modern Middle School and have invited Yi Peiji and Fan Xianyun to be directors. All preparations have been completed, and an application has been submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau for approval and filing. Enrollment information will be published in the newspaper soon.

Unprecedented Swimming Competition in Shanghai: Triangular Style Between China, Japan, and the United States

▲ A total of nine events

丨This Saturday at 8 PM at the Western Youth Association Swimming Pool丨

The triangular swimming competition between China, Japan, and the United States is scheduled to be held this Saturday at 8 PM at the Western Youth Association Swimming Pool in Jing'an Temple. The association considers this move to be unprecedented in Shanghai and will surely cause a sensation throughout the city. There are not many seats by the pool, with a fixed number of 250 seats. Tickets are priced at one yuan per person. Mr. Shen Siliang, honorary director of the YMCA, has been invited to serve as the chief referee. Mr. Hoer of the Seamen's Western Youth Association will be the starter. The scoring method is as follows: first place, 5 points; second place, 3 points; third place, 2 points; fourth place, 1 point; relay, 5, 3, and 1 points. The strength of all three sides is considerable. If the Chinese athletes can participate enthusiastically, the results will be excellent. The United States has selected experts from the association and members of the association from the MacLaines team to form a strong and sharp team, hoping to compete with China and Japan. The Japanese team is organized by students from the Tongwen School and the Japanese Navy. There are nine events, listed on the left.

(1) 50-yard freestyle

(2) 100-yard backstroke

(3) 200-yard freestyle

(4) Diving competition

(5) 100-yard freestyle

(6) 880-yard freestyle

(7) 200-yard relay (four people)

(8) 100-yard breaststroke

(9) 150-yard (three people backstroke, breaststroke, and freestyle)

▲ Held in Zhenjiang from September 18 to 20

丨Counties should first hold them in August

Zhenjiang Communication: The Jiangsu Provincial Amateur Games is now scheduled to be held in Zhenjiang for three days from September 18 to 20. On the 21st and 22nd, athletes will be selected to participate in the National Games. At that time, male and female athletes from middle schools throughout the province can participate. The venue is the Provincial Sports Field in the South Gate of the provincial capital. The funding is 10,000 yuan (including travel expenses to Beijing). (Approximately Jiangsu Province) A total of 128 athletes will be selected to attend the National Games. The allocation is as follows:

Men's and women's track and field, men's all-around about 30 people, men's soccer, men's and women's tennis, men's and women's basketball, and men's and women's volleyball about 90 people. Before the provincial meeting, each county should first hold county amateur sports meetings in August. The deadline for registering for the National Games is September 26. The athletes selected by the provincial amateur meeting will stay in the province for practice after the closing ceremony, so that they can go to Beijing on the opening of the National Games on October 10.
