Shareholders of Hanyeping Warn Sheng Zecheng

▲Advocating for a Rigorous Investigation

According to the Guowen News Agency, the Hanyeping Coal and Iron Company, Limited, is a well-known enterprise in the country, with abundant mineral resources and a grand organizational structure, surpassing those of Japan and Russia. However, for decades, due to mismanagement, the full authority of the company has been transferred to the Japanese, and most of the Daye pig iron has been monopolized by them. Recognizing this situation, the shareholders jointly sent a warning letter to Mr. Sheng Zecheng, the company's manager, demanding the disclosure of information for reorganization. The letter reads: "To Whom It May Concern: The Hanyeping Coal and Iron Company, Limited, has been in operation for a considerable number of years, and the two share offerings totaled 30 million yuan, which is a significant investment. As the most famous mining industry in the country and a top-priority enterprise, it should benefit the nation and its people, and its ability to achieve extraordinary profits goes without saying. However, since its inception, Mr. Sheng has governed incompetently, allowing others to dominate and exploit the company. He has wholeheartedly used the production of the two mines to benefit our enemies. During the European War, coal and iron prices soared, but the company's management turned a blind eye and allowed the Japanese to buy pig iron and iron sand at the lowest prices, deceiving the nation and its people in a shocking manner. The losses incurred are immeasurable. Although the manipulation originated with the Japanese, collusion occurred within the management. They disregarded the shareholders and the country's interests. Since then, the company's management has become increasingly bold, granting full authority to the Japanese. The mine management is now under the control of the Yawata Iron Works, and the company's accounting is handled by the Japanese Imperial Government. The company deceives itself and others by paying them salaries, acting as accomplices to the enemy. The coal and iron industry is related to the rise and fall of national power. Therefore, the company's articles of association prohibit foreign shares. The late Premier Sun Yat-sen also emphasized this in his plans for national development. The National Government claims to be governed by the party and follows the teachings of the late Premier in all its measures, protecting coal and iron mines with utmost care. However, you have inherited the legacy and continued the practice of ceding national rights and inviting wolves into the house. While this may be beneficial to you, what about the shareholders? What about the country? Furthermore, the Japanese loan case has historically involved unfair low prices. During the European War, they made huge profits, which has been publicly criticized by people in Japan. According to international morality, the Japanese government has no right to say anything other than to relinquish the loan. However, you, as a Chinese citizen and a key member of the company, have failed to argue on principle, allowing the Japanese to usurp our position and acting as a puppet. What face do you have to meet the elders of the country? What is even more hateful is that the Daye mine is world-renowned, and its interests are not limited to the shareholders. The endless treasures are being surrendered to the Japanese. For decades, the annual output of ore to the Yawata Iron Works has been over 400,000 to 500,000 tons. These important raw materials are supplied to the Japanese without corresponding compensation. Even if you do not leave any room for the country, shouldn't you think about future generations? The Japanese loan agreement and the purchase contract are private actions that the shareholders cannot recognize. The shareholders have a duty to oppose the Japanese control of the company's full authority. For more than ten years, no official profits have been received, and the shares are now worthless. Furthermore, the company's accounts have not been reported, and the shareholders' meeting exists only in name, with no meetings ever convened. All of these matters fall within your scope of authority, and you should be questioned about them. Regarding the above items, we request that you provide a clear response within ten days and make it public. If you fail to do so, we will disclose the entire case and seek a just resolution through legal means. We hereby inform you and hope you will consider this. Sincerely, shareholders of Hanyeping Coal and Iron Company, Limited, Qiu Jiao Ji, Li Shen Shouting, etc. Communication address: Law Office of Feng Kan, 106 Sichuan Road."

Yongjia Medical Association Requests Measures to Prevent the Spread of Fujian Plague into Wenzhou

▲Letter to the National Seaport Quarantine Service

Dr. Wu Liande, Director of the National Seaport Quarantine Service at 2 Jiujiang Road, yesterday received a letter from the Yongjia Medical Association of Zhejiang, stating, "To Whom It May Concern: We recently learned from the Xiamen news column in the Shanghai Shibao of July 6th that the plague in southern Fujian is rampant, with outbreaks in Xiangtian Village in Xianyou County, Hanjiang Town in Putian County, Yan Nian Guan Xiamen Port, Foyun District in Zhangpu County, and Xinqiao Tou Rice Market Street in Zhangzhou, causing hundreds of deaths in succession, and there are not enough coffins to purchase, etc. Fujian Province borders southern Zhejiang. In recent years, sea transportation has become increasingly convenient, with ships arriving in the morning and evening. If the plague spreads, Pingyang's Ao River, Ruian's Feiyun River, and Yongjia's Ou River will all be entry points. In the past, the plague in Fujian Province spread to Pingyang, but fortunately, transportation was obstructed at the time, and the impact was quickly eliminated. Today, however, sea and land transportation is very different from the past, and the speed and extent of its spread are self-evident. Your office should have carefully investigated the details reported in the newspaper. If the situation is true, then for the sake of taking precautions, strict inspections should be carried out on ships traveling to and from the ports of Pingyang, Ruian, and Yongjia. These areas have never had formal quarantine agencies. Therefore, during the large-scale cholera and meningitis outbreaks in recent years, no quarantine officials were found to be diligently performing their duties. This association, in light of the past neglect of seaport quarantine and the fear of future plague transmission, must ask your office to take early measures to ensure the well-being of the people and eliminate hidden dangers. As this matter concerns urgent epidemic prevention, this letter is sent for your information and attention, and to strengthen our public duty."

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Certifies Huachang Paint

▲Subjected to Chemical Testing by the Hygiene Testing Laboratory

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent an official letter to the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Civil Affairs yesterday regarding the case against Li Guohua of Huachang Manufacturing Factory, stating, "To Whom It May Concern: Our chamber previously saw a local news item in Hangzhou, which stated that over two hundred cans of health paint from the Hangzhou branch of Shanghai Huachang Paint Factory were seized and, after chemical testing by the Department of Civil Affairs, were confirmed to be opium substitutes. As the factory is a member of our chamber, the reported incidents indirectly affect the reputation of commercial organizations. We inquired with the factory about the situation and requested a detailed response. On the 22nd of this month, we received a reply from Huachang Factory, which stated, 'The health paint produced by our factory is made from useless scraps of leather and chemical solutions and does not contain opium. In July of the 18th year of the Republic of China, it was submitted to the Central Hygiene Testing Laboratory for testing, which confirmed that it was oil and issued Notification No. 24, which was received by our factory as proof. Furthermore, when our oil is exported, it is inspected by customs. If it contained opium, would customs allow it to pass? This time, the Zhejiang Department of Civil Affairs identified the health paint sold by the Hangzhou branch as an opium substitute and has detained and interrogated the manager of our branch, Huang Liquan, and Li Shengqing. Officials from Zhejiang have also been dispatched to Shanghai to investigate the factory together with Western officials from the Public Works Department. The Western officials declared on the spot that the paint produced by our factory did not contain any toxic substances and that the concession authorities had approved its operation. The officials from Zhejiang were speechless and withdrew. Therefore, the paint produced by our factory, according to the above-mentioned sales procedures and the statement of the Public Works Department officials, is purely made from scientific compounds and does not contain any toxic substances. It is evident. If the Zhejiang Department of Civil Affairs is raising the issue, what is the truth? Fortunately, the managers of our branch have been detained and are awaiting investigation, and the truth will come out. However, in today's world, it is difficult to guarantee that there will be no framing or false accusations. This must be solemnly declared and brought to your attention. We also implore you to forward this to the Zhejiang Department of Civil Affairs for an impartial investigation to avoid fabrication and to serve public justice, etc.' Attached are copies of the Central Hygiene Testing Laboratory's chemical testing certificate and the customs registration certificate. The health paint produced by Huachang Paint Factory has been tested by the Central Hygiene Testing Laboratory and confirmed to be oil without any toxic substances, with a certificate as proof. Furthermore, the products are exported and inspected by customs. If they were indeed opium substitutes, how could they be easily released? Moreover, the Public Concession has strict prohibitions on opium and has never allowed the manufacture of drugs. The factory's statement is credible. The sudden discovery of substitutes in the Hangzhou branch is suspected to be something else. Based on the above, we have enclosed copies of the chemical testing certificate and the customs registration certificate for your information."

Free Talk

Words of Wisdom

— Hanman

▲Sun Guoting said: "Only with the beauty of Nan Wei can one discuss She Yuan; only with the sharpness of Longquan can one discuss cutting." But generally, people often lack these abilities and like to make unfounded criticisms or act recklessly.

▲Whenever one feels depressed and bored, grind an inkstone of ink, take a stack of paper, and copy a favorite stone inscription by the window. This will resolve the sorrow and pain.

▲Being ignorant oneself and resenting those who are learned—this is speaking for the jealous. Seeking only one's own benefit and disregarding the opinions of others—this is speaking for the shameless.

▲Poison in a delicacy will never be eaten by those who know.

▲Love is like eating ginger candy: sweet at first, then spicy.

▲Most divorces occur because one party has already found someone else.

▲The currently popular long qipao for women has a stiff, high collar and a tight, small hem, resembling a yoke and shackles.

▲If regarding virtuous mothers and good wives as shameful for modern women, then the crisis of the nation will lie here in the future.

▲Love is the most treasured and secret thing at the center, and also the thing most desired to be shown to others. All suicides by lovers are merely a way to tell people things that cannot be said.

Physiological Advantages of Women

— Lü Bing

In the eyes of the Chinese, women seem to be weak and men are mostly strong. While this is not a universal truth, women who are physically stronger than men are in the minority. Unexpectedly, according to a recent publication by a German university professor, women are physiologically superior to men. This is quite a surprising statement and worthy of study.

The German professor's praise for women is based on the fact that women, on average, have a richer supply of vitamins than men. He gathered a large number of men and women and conducted a public experiment not long ago. The results showed that among the 330 people who lacked vitamins, only 38 were women. The professor also said that women's clothing is generally thinner than men's. For example, in severe cold weather, they wear light furs and only silk stockings on their feet, without fear of the cold. This is enough to show that strong muscles are an advantage for women. However, women may feel suspicious upon hearing this, thinking that more vitamins often lead to obesity, which is not aesthetically pleasing. In fact, this is not entirely true. The vitamins contained in women are deeply embedded in the muscles beneath the skin and develop faster than in men. Furthermore, aided by high-heeled shoes, women use their toes to exert force and sway their entire body, which is a natural exercise that prevents excessive muscle fat. It also maintains the beauty that women should possess. As for men, who do not have excessive vitamins, there is no need to perform similar exercises when walking. According to the professor's research, baldness in humans is a phenomenon caused by brain development. This is not related to the topic, so I will not elaborate.

Perils of Traveling in Siberia (4)

— Ping

▲Poor Diet: Food in the train is inedible. Seventy-seven meal tickets are given each day, providing four meals, consisting only of a few slices of sandy black bread, beefsteak, stinky fish, and sauerkraut soup, which are rotated in turn. All of them are mixed with ash and sand, not only bland and tasteless but also extremely dirty and expensive. For example, a plate of beefsteak costs US$1.40 (more than RMB 5), and an egg costs US$0.15. Even milk and butter are sour and smelly. It is better to endure hunger than to eat and get sick. Several Western friends traveling with Mr. Cao fell ill on the way, all due to poor diet.

▲White Russian Harassment: After the train departs, passersby along the way will throw stones and mud at the windows and passengers. The glass in the dining car and bedrooms is shattered, injuring passengers. This happened eight times in seven days in Russia. Some passengers were hit and bled from the head, some had their glasses broken, and a Western woman was injured in the waist and vomited blood. The reason given is that unemployed White Russians are using this as a way to vent their anger, which is the ultimate in boredom.

▲Confiscation of Equipment: The Red Russians consider items such as cameras, typewriters, telescopes, phonographs, and radios that travelers carry with them to be the possessions of capitalists and confiscate them according to old regulations. Now, they impose import taxes, which are almost arbitrary. However, photographic negatives must be developed by customs officers upon departure and are sometimes confiscated as well, for fear of exposing the inside story after the Red Russian autocracy.

▲Heavenly Bliss: As soon as travelers enter Manchuria, they feel like they have returned home. Everyone's faces are filled with smiles. After suffering all the way, we were all thin and exhausted. On the day of changing trains at the Sino-Russian border, everyone congratulated each other. Chinese customs officials and railway police also greeted us with smiles. We felt like we had broken through heavy encirclement, escaped from a tiger's den, and entered Penglai, ascending to a fairyland. The joy cannot be described in words.

Trivial Talk About Summer Lotus

— Yang Yixiao

▲Lotus Tea: When the lotus flower first blooms, take a small handful of fine tea leaves and wrap them in thin paper. Place them in the flower and take them out the next morning. Brew tea with it for a fresher and more delicious taste.

▲Lotus Dew: In the summer, collect lotus dew. The method is to use a bamboo pole to lift a clean towel and collect the dew from the lotus pond. When the towel is wet, wring it tightly into a container. The taste is sweet, and it can relieve summer heat.

▲Lotus Congee: Stew congee in a casserole and add a lotus leaf with its stem. Once the congee begins to boil, remove the lotus leaf. The color will be greenish and the aroma will fill your mouth.

▲Lotus Petals: Take the petals of a white lotus flower that are newly opened and without blemishes. Mix them with egg white and flour, then fry them in hot oil until both sides are yellow. Add a little white sugar on top. They are fragrant, crispy, and delicious.

The Empty Coffin Scheme

— Huang Yingdai

There was a certain Mr. Zhang, a modern youth. He had studied in Shanghai and, after graduating, took a job in an agency in Tianjin. He then took his family north. His wife was also a modern woman. The couple lived in a rented house in Tianjin and enjoyed all the pleasures of a modern family. Zhang, after losing his wife, experienced the pain of being a widower. Later, he received a telegram from his wife's family, instructing him to transport the coffin back to the South. However, Zhang's income in Tianjin was not high. During their life together, he and his wife could barely make ends meet. Transporting the coffin south from Tianjin would cost no less than a thousand yuan. He was unfamiliar with the area and had no way to raise such a large sum of money. Therefore, he decided to cremate his beloved wife. Using the latest electric cremation method, the body was reduced to ashes in fifteen minutes and placed in a tin box. He planned to take the box south. However, his wife's family had old-fashioned ideas. If he mentioned cremation, they would definitely object. Later, they repeatedly sent telegrams urging Zhang to transport the coffin back. Zhang was helpless. Moreover, they were relatives, and he feared hurting their feelings. Therefore, he devised an empty coffin scheme. In advance, he took the tin box south. After arriving in Shanghai, he bought an empty coffin and placed the tin box and his wife's favorite belongings in it. He deposited it in the funeral parlor of a certain public office. Then, he reported to his wife's family that the coffin had been transported back and was deposited in the funeral parlor. Upon hearing the news, his wife's family went to the public office to pay their respects. His mother-in-law even hugged the coffin and cried bitterly, unable to contain her grief. She did not know that the coffin was empty, containing only a box of ashes.

Terrible Flood

— Yu

In these past few years, the Chinese people have suffered all kinds of disasters, such as war, drought, banditry, and countless others. The afflicted areas often spanned several vast provinces, and the periods of suffering often stretched for years. The number of deaths was uncountable, and even now, it has not ended. The people in the disaster areas still do not know when they will be able to escape from the fires and waters and find peace. Unexpectedly, a new kind of flood, unprecedented and affecting an even wider area, has begun to wreak havoc. The extent of the damage in the future cannot yet be predicted. The hearts of people everywhere are filled with indescribable panic. Alas, Heaven is merciless to this extent; what else can be said? If you ask how vast the disaster area is, then it can be said that there is no place, north, south, east, or west, that is not likely to be affected. Both the northern and southern capitals, the old and new, have shown signs of disaster. After a heavy thunderstorm on the first day of this month in Beiping, the electricity and telephone lines were all blown down. The whole city was pitch black, and three people were struck and killed by lightning. Countless houses were destroyed. The water on the streets was ankle-deep, a vast expanse of water, turning the city into a swamp. The Yongding River rose sharply by twenty feet, exceeding ground level by five feet. The water was only about a foot away from the top of the embankment, and there was a risk of collapse at any moment. Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang specially ordered engineers to camp on the embankment to guard against it day and night. The surrounding farmland has also turned into a vast expanse of water. Even if there is no more heavy rain, the Yongding River will remain intact, but the autumn harvest is hopeless. In Nanjing, there has also been torrential rain in the past week. Water accumulated on the streets, reaching shin-deep. Many other places are also suffering from flooding, showing signs of becoming a disaster. Taking these two capitals, old and new, as examples, one can imagine the rest. Yesterday, I met a friend from Gaoyou, and only then did I learn that the floods in the northern Jiangsu area were particularly severe. When this friend left Gaoyou, most of the people's homes had already been flooded. More than a thousand houses had collapsed from being submerged. The Grand Canal rose sharply to fourteen feet. People were in a state of panic day and night, not even having time to sleep or eat. Because to the west of the Grand Canal, separated only by an embankment, is West Lake, which is over four hundred li long and connects to Hongze Lake in the north. If there is more heavy rain, the embankment will not be reliable. Once the embankment breaks, all the land in Gaoyou County will be connected to West Lake. All the people are in danger of being buried in the bellies of fish. Shanghai has had several consecutive days of heavy rain. I don't know what the situation is like in Gaoyou now. My hometown is certainly also a concern. Half a month ago, the newspaper reported that the Baojia Dam almost collapsed. I have also heard people say that there is water on the city walls as well. Then, the flooding of the surrounding farmland is self-evident. Moreover, the steamer to Zhenjiang has been suspended for many days. News is cut off, so I can't even receive letters from home. I don't know what the extent of the disaster is. As the saying goes, "water and fire are merciless." But the disaster of water has great universality. A fire only affects one place, so how can they be compared? Alas, a terrible flood.

▲ News from the Art World: Mr. Zhao Junmin of Shaoxing, whose given name is Nengzhang, is a nephew of Mr. Huishu. He indulged in the six methods of painting from a young age, with a family tradition of scholarship. He especially immersed himself deeply in painting flowers, adhering to a style that is both vigorous and graceful. Later, he traveled to Shanghai with his uncle, Mr. Xuehou, and resided at 16 Dongpushi Road in the French Concession. Many seek his art there.

Travel Notes from India (67)

— Linghua

On the morning of March 1st, a student named Krishna, about sixteen years old, invited me to visit the Golden Temple of Hinduism. It is a famous temple in Varanasi. For several days, he urged me to go, saying that I must go to see the essence of Hinduism. We walked there, about three li. We passed through narrow alleys, with many twists and turns, where carriages and horses could not pass. Gradually, I saw many old philosophers with their faces painted in various colors coming out of the alleys. I knew that we were not far from the Golden Temple. There were many poor people begging for money. If you gave money to one, they would surround you, so I dared not give any. At the entrance to a narrow alley, I suddenly saw a large, gray-white creature with two horns on its head coming out of the alley. Everyone touched their foreheads with their hands and said, "This is a divine creature." I looked at it and saw that it was a gray-white cow. I respectfully made way and let the sacred cow pass. There was also a small sacred cow following it. The alley was narrow, and the body of a sacred cow blocked the way, leaving no room for pedestrians. There were many men and women, and it was very crowded. The ground was covered with mud and flowers. Suddenly, someone stopped me and asked, "Who is this person? Can he enter the Hindu temple?" The student said, "This is a Chinese Buddhist." He sprinkled water on my head, and then I was allowed to pass. Everyone who passes must have water sprinkled on them. We went further to the temple gate. I had to take off my shoes. I saw a well with various kinds of flowers scattered in it. There were people selling flowers. You had to have flower water sprinkled on your head before you could enter. There was also a gatekeeper who would not allow me to enter. He saw that the hat I was wearing was Western-style and said that I was a Christian. The student explained for a long time before I was allowed to enter. It is said that even Hindus from distant lands are sometimes not allowed to enter. Its sacredness is so difficult to behold. I held flowers and entered barefoot with the crowd. The ground was muddy. In the temple, I only saw many people crowding around a flower water altar. In the center of the water was a yin-yang stone, which is the sacred object I described earlier, depicting the sexual union of male and female organs. The crowd surrounded it and received baptism. However, all four walls of the room were hung with mirrors, reflecting countless people receiving baptism here. I knew that there was a method in hypnotism called the full-room mirror hypnosis method. Entering it, there were too many people, and I couldn't squeeze through. The people's clothes were all unclean. I was very afraid of being crowded, but the guide insisted on letting me receive the grace of the flower water. He dragged me and squeezed me up. I wanted to laugh but couldn't. Soon I came out. This was receiving the baptism of the Golden Temple. I had previously participated in Muslim worship with Muslims. This time, I participated in the baptism of the Hindu yin-yang religion. I am simply studying limitless methods. Playing with the rituals of life, there are limitless beings. How dare I criticize them severely?

About a li away from the Golden Temple, I reached the banks of the Ganges River. The morning sun rose in the east, and the river water was clear. The scenery was very beautiful, unlike the turbid Ganges in Calcutta. However, men and women were still bathing in the muddy water, seeking liberation. This water was clear and rippled, with small boats swaying back and forth. Suddenly, a large head emerged from the waves, shaped like a human head. I asked in surprise what it was. They said, "It's a big fish." I asked if anyone fished here. They answered that no one eats fish in this sacred city. The big fish also do not eat people. After passing this place, in other places, Muslims fish and eat fish. The big fish also eat people. Here, the big fish are allowed to come and go freely and do not harm people. I seemed to believe the student's words, which made sense. It was similar to what a certain professor said yesterday, that Gandhi mourned for people who killed tigers and snakes. It is the principle of cause and effect. If two do not harm each other, then they forget each other. The people of Xuzhou in the north like to eat dog meat, so dogs often eat dead people. The elders in my hometown say that the people of Jiangnan do not eat dog meat, so when coffins are left in the wild for a long time, dogs do not eat the dead. The elders say that this is so. I think it is the same principle as the one the child discussed, that the people of Varanasi do not eat fish, and the fish do not eat people. I am not yet fully convinced of this because I have the principles of science in my mind. I also half believe in this scientific cause-and-effect talk of religion.

The Rotary Club Storytelling

??? (31)

— Xu Zhuodai

"You can't? You can't catch bedbugs, so you can be my husband?"

"What a joke! Does your husband have to be able to catch bedbugs?"

"It's not just my husband, anyone who can't catch bedbugs is not fit to be anyone's husband!"

Ziliang was extremely angry, he stood there and did not go to catch them.

"Then, when our father-in-law and mother-in-law choose a son-in-law, why not first hold a bedbug-catching contest, see who catches the most, and marry their daughter to him?"

"This is not my creation. I heard that there is a yarn factory in Hangzhou where the workers were complaining about bedbugs in the dormitory, so the manager suddenly issued an order saying that all staff, large and small, and even the workers, who could not catch bedbugs would be suspended from work. Sure enough, as soon as this order was issued, everyone worked hard to catch them, and before long, they completely eradicated the bedbugs. Several people who really couldn't catch them were fired at the end of the month. Someone went to plead for them, but the manager said: 'If a person can't even catch bedbugs, what else can they do? Are they fit to be workers?' Judging from the manager's words, it can be seen that catching bedbugs is a very easy task in life, so you, as a husband, must also be able to do it. If you can't, you can also be suspended from work!"

After saying that, she laughed again.

"This is what the manager said to the workers, not what a woman said to her husband."

"A husband is also a kind of worker!"

Ziliang knew that the more he said, the more wrong it would be, so he might as well go and catch some, just to get by. He first lit a candle, walked to the bed, opened the pillow, and luckily for Ziliang, he saw a big bedbug scurrying there.

Commercial News

Financial Gold Market Storm Rises Suddenly

▲ A Difference of Twenty-Three Taels in Half a Day: Yesterday, the 23rd, the Gold Exchange held a memorial service for the tragic incident involving overseas Chinese in Korea, so it was closed for half a day in the morning. When business resumed as usual in the afternoon, the gold price rose and fell repeatedly, changing drastically. The wild storm could not be contained. From noon to evening, there was a difference of twenty-three taels. People were panicked. In the end, it fell by more than six taels. It seems that the silver market fell, and American stocks also declined, so the gold price immediately soared, suddenly exceeding the 750-tael mark. Buyers were quite strong. Afterwards, it was suddenly heard that Germany was borrowing money from the United States, which was hopeful, and buying silver to mint silver coins to supplement the financial system. People were immediately terrified. Many large bullish traders tended to sell. Then, the exchange rate also weakened, and a big wave arose, plummeting twenty taels, giving the impression that the sky was shaking. It finally reached 732 or 33 taels. Afterwards, buyers seemed to become active, and a peaceful atmosphere returned.

▲ Unofficial Trading Before Noon: From before noon, a small number of colleagues had been trading unofficially outside the exchange, with prices ranging from 751 or 52 taels to 55 taels, then back to 51 or 52 taels. The big news had not yet changed. The silver price fell by a small eighth, and private telegrams also fell by a sixteenth, so people's hearts were high. However, the exchange rate quotation did not change, only adding 25 to the Japanese gold price.

▲ The Opening Price in the Afternoon Jumped More Than Eight Taels: The official opening price in the afternoon was 54 taels and 5 qian, which was 8 taels and 2 qian higher than yesterday's closing price. Next was 55 taels and 2 qian. Dalian Trading Company and exchange rate arbitrage firms were buying. It seems that British gold could be settled at 125 to 0625. Soon after, Yuancheng, Tong Taichang, Yingfenghang, etc. sold, falling back by more than four taels. At 2:10 pm, it was 50 taels and 05 qian, and British gold could be settled at 125. Soon after, Mitsui ate 125 to 1875. Banks traded interbank transactions for this month at 125 to 2:30 pm at 52 and a half taels.

▲ Hopes for German Debt, a Plunge of Twenty Taels: Afterwards, a storm suddenly arose. Rumors spread that German debt had been settled and that they wanted to buy silver. Large traders such as Bingxing, Yuanxingyong, Qianchangxiang, and speculators sold one after another. Bullish traders were eager to get rid of their holdings. Bearish traders worked hard to add to their positions. Also, goods were also being sold off. Consequently, the price broke through 50 taels and continued to fall, seemingly unstoppable. In a moment, it plummeted another ten taels or more. The price of British gold was being sold by colleagues to various banks at prices as low as 3125 to 375. Therefore, at 3 pm, it was finally 32 taels. Dalian gangs and others took advantage of this to chase the price, and it was heard that HSBC was eating 3125, so it pulled up another seven or eight taels to 40 taels. However, the selling wind did not stop and remained weak. It fell by more than five taels. At 3:30 pm, it was 30 and a half taels.

▲ Evening Recovery, Still Up Six Taels and Seven Qians: From 4 pm, it recovered and rose again. Buyers were strong again. Yuan Maoyong, Wanxing, Tong Taichang, etc. pulled in a lot, and the price was raised by six taels. Near the close, it was 40 taels and 05 qian. At 4:30 pm, the closing price was 39 and a half taels, then it rose another three taels, to more than 42 taels to three taels. Compared to the day before (according to the listed price), it still fell by six taels and seven qian. The maximum price in half a day was 55 taels and 2 qian, and the minimum price was 32 taels, a swing of 23 taels and 2 qian. The volatility of the market made people feel at a loss.

▲ Raw Silver Adds Only Ten Taels and Two Qians and Five Lis: The opening price for goods was 54 taels and 5 qian, and the closing price was 40 taels and 05 qian. The listed price was changed to 792 taels and 6 qian, subtracting 40 to 60 taels, then back to 52 or 3 taels. The book price was 38 to 40 taels. Supplementary water was 38 taels. The raw silver seemed to be softening, adding only ten taels and two qians and five lis. Yingfenghang sold more than 1,000 taels to Tianjin and Dalian gangs because those gangs, seeing the sharp drop in the gold price, thought the raw silver was small and profitable, so they immediately acted. Also, Hankou gangs and silver shops sold several hundred taels to Yingfenghang at a price of ten taels and two qians and five lis.

▲ Chaotic Market, Difficult to Investigate In and Out: As for the transactions of various firms on the trading floor, they were extremely complicated and the volume was quite high. Because the market was extremely chaotic and the changes were dramatic, it was difficult to investigate. However, according to statistics, Yuan Maoyong, Wanxing, Tong Taichang, Shunli, etc. were all buying positions. Bingxing, Yuanxingyong, Yuantai, Yu Da, and goods were all selling. Qianchangxiang, Zhifenghang, Cuichangyong, Yuanheng, Futaiheng, Yuanchun, Yuankangxiang, Longsheng, Yuhe, etc. were in and out in a very complicated manner. Also, those who specialized in exchange rate arbitrage came in and out repeatedly. The Dalian gangs bought a total of more than 7,000, sold more than 1,000, and the Guangdong gangs had few transactions.

Youth Corner

Haste Makes Waste

—Du Mei

"Haste makes waste," "A fine net catches no fish," all similar aphoristic idioms, I have gradually come to believe now. This is not for any special reason, but simply because I am getting older and have more experience, which naturally gives me more insights. I don't feel happy about it; I only feel that my childlike innocence is gradually disappearing. The life of simply enjoying the shade under a big tree has been implicitly declared bankrupt. Although I don't need to weather any great storms or resist any huge waves, I still need to take care of things within a certain range. Alas, the days of playing all day, when the oil bottle falling over was none of my business, I'm afraid I can only dream of now. The scenes before the age of sixteen constantly ripple in my mind, but youth and innocence are constantly repelling each other, going in opposite directions. Detestable youth increases relentlessly, second by second, while the precious "innocence" is invisibly eroded and destroyed by it. What can't be pushed away is youth, but what can't be kept is innocence, alas, where has it disappeared to?

My sister's marriage is a very good example. Although her husband's family is one of the best in the area, she is already the mother of two children after four or five years. Those adorable babies, alas, are the main reason for the disappearance of her youth. And when I think of our mother, raising the seven of us sisters, even if a person is cast from iron, they would have to be polished bright, right? Not to mention anything else, even I, as an older sister, have been worried and tired for a ten-year-old younger sister, starting from the recent past. Now, I am also taking on the responsibility of caring for my younger brother.

My younger sister was brought here by me in the first month of this year to attend school. Because she was too young and away from her loving mother's embrace for the first time, and most importantly, she didn't understand the local language. She didn't understand others, and others didn't understand her even more. She not only spoke a pure local dialect but also mixed in many colloquialisms that young children have but adults rarely use. In this situation, living at school was impossible, so she lived in my dormitory. Every day, I had to take her to the attached elementary school of the Patriotic Girls' School near my school. Fortunately, Patriotic Girls' School is my alma mater, so there was still a place to take care of her. But for the past six months, I have taken care of her daily life, whether she was hungry or cold, especially when she was sick not long after arriving. The food was too bad, and she wasn't used to eating it, leaving me at a loss. At that time, I felt like I had been startled and thought about the hardship my mother endured raising me and the others, from babies of eight inches to growing up so big, and then educating us. What a tremendous labor that is! Then I made a new resolution: my mother's kindness should be repaid one by one. Alas, great and benevolent mothers of the world, your contribution to humanity is so exquisite and outstanding!

Recently, although my younger sister has returned, my younger brother has come. I can say that I have transplanted the heart of caring for my younger sister onto him. He can't eat the local food very well. Within the realm of what is possible, I always have to find a way to make him eat. Fine, as a result, I have to eat lunch before I can go out. In the afternoon, I have to rush back to school before six o'clock; otherwise, I will be uneasy. The time I spend outside, especially when I tell him to wait for me but cannot get back on time, makes me even more anxious. Yesterday was like this: "Brother, I'm going out. Be sure to wait for me to come back for dinner." "Okay, I'll wait for you."

It was also to finish writing a manuscript, so I was so engrossed that I didn't care that I had spent too much time. The boarder had already sent the food. Friends asked me to eat before leaving, but how could I? I hurriedly gathered my papers, umbrella, grabbed them, and ran. While changing cars, I bought some snacks, which inevitably delayed me a little. When I got to the North Station, I was hungry and didn't care to look to see if it was Route 3 or Route 1 public bus. I hurriedly jumped on, bought a ticket, and felt a little relieved. In less than a quarter of an hour, I would be able to get to school. It wasn't too late at six-thirty. While my chaotic thoughts had not yet settled down, the ticket inspector came to check my ticket, interrupting my mixed thoughts. The bus gradually turned westward. I knew things were a little bad. It was going to go back to the factory to add "Vaseline," which would delay me a few more minutes. This again caused the impatience and anxiety that had just been interrupted.

"Hey, Miss Jin, are you going to Zhenru?"

"No, back to school." The voice was familiar to me. Without looking up, I determined that it was Mr. Xu, who works in the bus company. I casually responded to him like this.

"Oh, you're wrong. How did you get on Route 3? I thought you were going to Zhenru."

"Oh, I wasn't paying attention. This is really absurd. I've never been this confused before. I was so anxious that I got confused. I'm glad you saw me." I felt extremely ashamed, and anxiety and irritability intensified, pressing in on my mind. At this time, I was extremely resentful. Why was I so careless? Even if people don't laugh at me for being illiterate, they'll laugh at me for being too careless.

"Okay, it doesn't matter. Please stay on this bus, get off outside the factory, and transfer again." Mr. Xu and the familiar ticket collector, seeing my anxious and remorseful expression, both said this to me, as if containing a tone of comfort. And the ticket collector also said to Mr. Xu, "You put her on the bus and tell the ticket seller that this ticket is valid."

In this process, of course, I had already switched to a different route bus. Mr. Xu waited with me on Qiujiang Road for a long time before seeing a bus come that was marked "1," but it was going to Zhenru. So, we waited again. Luckily, not a moment later, another "1" came, but it wasn't going to Jiangwan. It was marked "Entering Factory" below, and there were no passengers inside. As a result, a total of four buses passed by. At five minutes per bus, five times four is twenty minutes that had passed. Besides the first bus that went to the factory to add "Vaseline," I also had to switch to another bus. By calculation, it was certainly more than twenty minutes. I kept waiting until the fifth bus went. Who knew it would go to the factory again? This time it wasn't to "add Vaseline," but to replace a new horn. At the same time, the drivers and ticket sellers were laughing and joking with each other. But how could they know that I, as a passenger, was burning with anxiety?

When I returned to school, it was already 7:45, a total loss of forty minutes. I then deeply felt that "haste makes waste" and "a fine net will never catch fish," which invisibly gave me a lesson.

Ms. Wu Wenjing

— Bing She

Daughter of the Gatekeeper

— Yu Xi

The gatekeeper of our school is a tall Northerner, surnamed Cai. People all call him Old Cai, because he is a bit old, but his spirit is still that of a young man. His face is ruddy, and a kind smile is always hanging at the corners of his eyes. His mature and prudent attitude is admirable.

Page 22

He came to work as a gatekeeper at the beginning of our school's founding. During this time, the school has gone through many vicissitudes, and the principals have been replaced many times. The students are transformed every year, the old go and the new come, like travelers. Even the teachers, there is not one who taught at our school twenty years ago and is still at our school. Only him, the gatekeeper, has never been transferred. His history as the gatekeeper of our school is as long as the school's life history. He is our authority on the past. Sometimes when he talks to students or anyone about the various situations of the school in the past, he is as enthusiastic as an eighty- or ninety-year-old man telling children about the "Longhairs" (Taiping rebels).

His salary is the highest among the school workers. The students also have a good impression of him. At the end of each semester, some would give him one or two dollars as a reward for delivering letters. After working diligently and frugally for many years, he must have quite a bit of savings. It is said that among all the school workers and the shopkeepers at the school gate, he is the wealthiest.

Everyone believes this.

But according to reliable investigation, the wealthiest among the school workers is Old Wang, the dormitory tea server, followed by the local errand runner surnamed Li. Old Cai only ranks third. Saying he is the richest is actually wronging him. But even if you wrong him, he doesn't get angry. He just smiles and says slowly, "Haha, everyone hopes so. It's just that things don't go as planned."

Sometimes he would then sigh, "These years, just the expenses of oil, salt, firewood, and rice at home are enough to make people struggle."

His home is at the school gate, consisting of three rooms in a one-story house. In front of the house, there is a candy store selling snacks and daily necessities. The business is quite good, but according to Old Cai himself, doing business with students is really difficult. If you don't give credit, the business is small. If you give credit, it's really exhausting to collect the debts. And no matter how tight you are, there will always be some losses in the accounts every year. "So for a store like mine," he said, "I am already very satisfied if I can make ends meet every year."

This is the truth. The students of our school come from all directions: Sichuan, Guangdong, the Northeast, and even overseas Chinese. They don't care about the cost of food and drink, but they like to buy on credit. For example, they say,

"Hey, one bread and one cup of coffee, write it down." Or they say,

"Hey, those two bottles of soda, put it on my tab."

At this time, who can say "No, you must pay now," or point to the red paper strip pasted on the wall that says "Thank you for your patronage, cash only"? Of course, you can only give them credit. Once you do, within half a year, they will unknowingly owe a lot of money. Some people, after owing money, won't think about paying until you ask them again and again. Or even if they do, they will postpone it to tomorrow, the day after tomorrow, or next week, until they can't postpone it any further. Then they will only pay you a few dollars and transfer a few dollars to the next account. Some even say they have no money to pay. When you encounter this kind of person, everyone wants to impound their luggage, which is a lot of trouble. In the end, it always ends up being handled carelessly...

At Old Cai's house, there are also his old wife and beloved daughter. The store also employs two assistants, making a total of five people eating. His daughter is studying at a nearby junior high school. That tuition fee is also something that our gatekeeper often calculates in his mind.

His daughter is only sixteen or seventeen years old. Because the place where she studies is close to home, she is a day student. She is very hardworking. According to several students in our school who are used to getting up early, every morning they can always hear her reading English aloud in her room. She reads for a while, then takes her schoolbag and goes to school. She doesn't come home until school is dismissed at four o'clock. After she comes home, she doesn't go out to play anywhere. She only helps her mother with chores such as washing clothes, washing rice, and washing vegetables. Sometimes she even sits in the store to help sell things and write accounts. If you don't see her in the store, and you don't see her on the river beach, then she must be in the bedroom doing math problems or practicing English composition.

She is petite, her face is also well-proportioned, and she is smart and lively. Therefore, the students of our school often like to use buying things as an excuse to get a chance to chat with her. This naive girl does not show any unwillingness. She talks to them, and sometimes she even asks them to explain the difficulties in her homework. At this time, the person being asked, regardless of whether he is an expert or a layman in this subject, cannot but readily agree to her request...

There are quite a few students in our school who act as her volunteer teachers.

This summer, she graduated from junior high school. She was first in her graduating class. This time, our school is enrolling students for the first time, and she came to apply for the first year of preparatory class. After reviewing the results, her ranking was also at the top. When her father saw his daughter's name on the list of newly admitted students to our school, he was overjoyed. He often said,

"This is with the help of the teachers." But how could he not have expected that his daughter would definitely be admitted? He has infinite hope for his daughter. He is willing to bear any burden for her to study and for her to seek happiness.

And Miss Cai is also giving her father a lot of glory. Not only is she good at her studies, but she has also shown her skills on the basketball court. In the junior high school she recently graduated from, she was the captain of the women's basketball team. Half a year ago, their women's team played against our school's women's team on our school's basketball court. At that time, she was playing defense.

We are glad that our school will have another female basketball player in the second half of the year...

When we occasionally talked about Miss Cai's admission to our school, someone joked, "Her father is a gatekeeper, so everything is cheap. The only thing she suffers from is that she can't exchange love letters with boys, haha."

Miss Hu Yi Nan

— Bing She

Social News

Britain Building the Largest Seaplane, Germany Dominates Land Planes with Superior Strength

— Jun Shan

To use an exaggerated phrase of the British, they rule the waves of the sea. This originally referred to ships, but since the rise of seaplanes, the proud British have refused to let anyone else seize the hegemony. Therefore, they are now building the world's largest seaplane, which is already under construction in South New Port.

This plane, once completed, will not only be the largest plane in the world, but also one of the most luxurious and prosperous. Although its shape and size are similar to Germany's largest DO-X, it can carry more passengers, has a higher speed, and is much more comfortable and luxurious. The name of this plane has not yet been announced. It is only known that it is being built by the Vickers company and is equipped with Rolls-Royce "Buzzard"

motors.

Its horsepower is equal to that of the Do-X, but it uses only six engines, while the Do-X uses twelve. Each engine has 1,000 horsepower and is installed in four seats on the plane's monoplane wing. The maximum speed can reach 145 miles per hour, and the normal speed is 120 miles per hour. This plane can carry forty passengers plus seven crew members. Passengers are not crammed together like most commercial planes. It is almost as comfortable as an American first-class parlor car. Each passenger has a spacious berth and a private room. The meals are also excellent, and there is a lookout room available.

This plane was ordered by the British Air Ministry. Although its purpose has not yet been announced, it is guessed that it is intended to fly to various colonies. The matter of flying from England to India, after the R-101 airship had problems, is about to be carried out.

Although it is made entirely of pure steel, this seaplane is extremely light and agile. When fully loaded with passengers, it can only fly one thousand miles, but if it is not carrying passengers, it can fly across the Atlantic Ocean safely without landing.

At the same time, we can also turn to the aspect of land planes. Undoubtedly, Germany occupies an unparalleled advantage. The largest land plane currently in use is a Junkers of the German Lufthansa, carrying passengers between Berlin and London. That plane can carry twenty people, including the crew.

The Life of Working Women in New York

— Lin

(7) A Glimpse of Life

Mamie has forty-five minutes for lunch. On very busy days, she is only allowed half an hour. This situation usually happens during the sales period, or perhaps on a few Saturdays and Sundays. Mamie must go to the changing room at noon, put on her coat, and then run out to find a place to eat. Her store has a dining room for employees, but Mamie and her colleagues prefer to eat outside the store at noon. The store's dining room is better and the food is not expensive. Running outside the store, they can find more places to eat. Mamie thinks fifteen minutes is enough to eat. Most of the time at noon, Mamie runs to a drugstore, stands outside the soda fountain and eats some sandwiches and ice cream. She often finds French pastries delicious. She would like to replace sandwiches with exquisite pastries. An Italian noodle shop sells a plate of hot noodles and a cup of coffee for twenty-five cents. Delicious cheese is placed on the table for free consumption. As for the variety of food in the snack bar, it is even more diverse. Mamie often feels that when she runs to these places, she overspends her meal allowance, because those foods are really mouthwatering. When eating, the girls often eat together. Salesgirls and packers have completely different statuses. Only after graduating from packing is a sales book given to her. This is Mamie's hope. She wants to be a salesgirl. Their salary can be as high as twenty dollars a week, and sometimes the commission is as much as four dollars. To be a salesperson, she must be eighteen years old and have experience in the store, or be promoted from the store.

When eating, the girls talk about nothing but store matters, and occasionally about personal matters, such as clothing issues, boyfriends, and family disagreements. They don't dawdle much when eating.

After the meal, everyone hurries back to the store to spend the long afternoon. The girls prefer to be busy, so that time passes easily. When the store is crowded with customers, they cannot rush home. Of course, during Christmas, the crowds of customers are terrible. When the girls go back, they are really too tired to move. During the Christmas season, they only have half an hour to eat, and they work all day without rest. Sometimes they even work overtime. According to New York's newly revised labor laws for working women, they cannot work too much overtime except for a fixed amount of time.

Mamie pays one dollar from her salary every month as an insurance fund and medical fund. She feels very stingy about this money and feels that it is paid after being forced. Many girls think this way, although a few people understand the benefits of this system.

During work hours in the store, knowledge is increased. There are several classes taught in the store, but the courses are all related to store organization and product knowledge. Very little is said about culture.

After the closing bell rings, probably at twenty minutes to six, the girls hurriedly cover the merchandise and rush to get their bags. If there are still many customers at that time, the bell cannot be rung to close the door until five thirty.

Mamie goes home, retracing the old path. At this time, the subway car is always unbearably crowded. Everyone breathes in bad air, and you push me and I push you in endless noise. Finally, Mamie arrives at her station and struggles to get out of the door. How cool and lovely is the air on the street! She loves the hazy street lights, which shine straight into Mamie's heart.

Finally, she arrives home. A hot and intense smell rushes into her nose, but she is hungry. Her mother has done a lot of hard work at home. The rent is forty-two dollars a month. Her father's money is very unreliable. When the family's economic situation is difficult, her mother has to go out to do odd jobs. She registers at a home service agency, so that she can find something to do when she needs work. Mamie gives half of her small monthly salary to her mother, and she keeps the remaining six dollars for transportation, meals, and clothing. She cannot be extravagant at all.

"Here comes Mamie," the girl shouts, "Now we can eat."

They don't eat in a fixed way. Dad hasn't come home yet. When it's late, he chatters endlessly with people, so the family no longer waits for him. Mamie swallows her food in one gulp.

"Mamie, why are you in such a hurry?" Rose asks.

"I have a date."

"Who are you dating?" Connie wants to know.

"Oh, Bert," Mamie gently taps her sister's head and rushes back to the bedroom to change clothes.

Bert is very young, a clerk in a store. He arrives at Mamie's place at about a quarter past eight. Mamie hasn't finished dressing yet. The girls are very shy when they see young men. They don't dare to talk to him. Mrs. Rochester is in the kitchen and doesn't come out. Finally, Mamie appears. She has dressed up very hard, looking like a wax doll, with blood-red lips, a face covered with white powder, and a lot of rouge on her cheeks. Her eyebrows and eyelashes are as black as a crow's wings. In short, as far as Mamie is concerned, she has put a lot of thought into her makeup to cope with a night gathering. She is wearing a black and tight-fitting dress, which makes her look even thinner.

Mamie and Bert run to the "Poppy Tots Club" to dance. This venue is organized by a group of young people who are still wet behind the ears. Each person pays two dollars to cover all the expenses of the dance floor and a three-person band. There are probably two hundred young men and women in the entire venue, and everyone's circumstances are about the same.

The music starts, Mamie's legs move faintly, and her boyfriend also waves non-stop.

"Come on, girl," Bert says as he spins her on the floor. Although the music is loud, it is not very in tune, but there is a kind of enthusiasm. In this place, many starving children find happiness and relieve all their boredom. (To be continued)
